## Monster Dice: Push ✅
*6 posts · started by MalphasVI on 2026-05-11* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3706716)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4610661` · 2026-05-11

Hello,
Anyone can tell me how the Monster Push dice work?

1. If my hero is next to a monster that is already closer to Grimheim than I am, do I still get affected by the monster’s “Push” effect? And if yes, in which direction am I pushed?
2. If a monster pushes me along its movement direction toward Grimheim, and this movement brings me into range of another monster, does that second monster also trigger its own Push effect on me?
3. If I am standing between two monsters (one on my left and one on my right), and Grimheim is to my right, how is the Push resolved?
Do I get pushed diagonally or in a specific direction?
Or do I not get pushed at all?


The rules say Push follows the monster’s path. If that path is blocked, does that mean the Push cannot be resolved at all? Or can the hero still be pushed in a different direction (for example diagonally) if that would bring them closer to Grimheim?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430994` · 2026-05-11

> ↳ *Replying to #1 (user `4610661`):* Hello, Anyone can tell me how the Monster Push dice work? 1. If my hero is next to a monster that is already closer to Grimheim than I am, do I still get affected by the monster’s “Push” effect? And if yes, in which dire…

> You only follow the monster move path towards Grimheim, and you are only pushed 1 step in total (or 0 steps if the way is blocked).
>
> Note that if you stand next to Grimheim you will be pushed into Grimheim, and the monsters may follow you in on their move step following the monster dice, making it risky to block the monsters so close to Grimheim.
>
> Cheers!

---
**#3** · user `4610661` · 2026-05-12 *(edited)*

That means that I could just make sure that I’m positioning myself anywhere around him except in his path to counter this. That is cool.
Thank you so much for the explanation.

I love the game.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430994` · 2026-05-12

> ↳ *Replying to #3 (user `4610661`):* That means that I could just make sure that I’m positioning myself anywhere around him except in his path to counter this. That is cool. Thank you so much for the explanation. I love the game.

> I think there is a misunderstanding. The only ways to not get pushed when that is rolled it to either 1) not be next to any monster, or 2) be unable to move towards Grimheim because the way is blocked by a monster, mountain, or other hero. The way is determined by the arrows at the edge of the board. It doesn't matter for the push if you block the monster or not.
> The push and the monsters movement are 2 separate things, so after the push roll has been resolved, all monsters move unless they then have a hero next to them or their way is blocked.

---
**#5** · user `2044257` · 2026-05-14

The developer already answered very clearly,  but I thought I could try to answer to your questions one by one trying to clarify things even more and hopefully helping people not fluent in english (like myself) to fully understand :-) . (If I got something wrong, I am sure the developers will intervene :-) ) 

1- Yes, you get affected unless this monster (or another monster) stands exactly at the one hex towards Grimheim (following the arrows) you would be pushed. So It does not matter at all if the monster is closer to Grimheim than your hero.

2- Every hero can only be pushed 1 hex per monster turn, so in your example only the first push would happen

3-If a hero stands at a certain position, you can only be pushed at one specific hex which is the next hex following the arrows towards Grimheim (same rules as monster move apply here). So, the exact number of monsters that are adjacent to you and their exact location does not really matter.

---
**#6** · user `4610661` · 2026-05-14

After Jacob’s second comment, I guessed so. But thank you so much for taking the time to explain it further.

---

## How does Wizard's Hat work?
*4 posts · started by Mad Math on 2026-04-16* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3694212)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1032765` · 2026-04-16

I assume you can use it only once per turn, because it's equipment. (There is a card that says "+1 to any die roll" but this one is fromulated differently, so that threw me off...)
I assume you may choose to use it after any diceroll.

Is this correct?

---
**#2** · user `1881095` · 2026-04-16

always post the card..

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2026-04-17

The Wizard hat allows you to always roll an extra dice when you roll dice. This applies to each attack, and each effect that rolls dice, not just once per turn.
I admit we should have made this clearer, but effects come in 2 forms:
1) "Imperatives": effects telling you to do something specific, like "Move 1 area." or "Put 1 damage here to roll 3 attack against an adajcent monster." Such effects can only be used once per turn, as per the rules.
2) State changes, triggers, and buffs. These are described more as changes to normal stats or rules, such as "When you perform an attack action, gain 1 XP.", or the Wizard's hat: "Whenever you roll attack, roll 1 more attack." These are not limited to once per turn.

---
**#4** · user `1032765` · 2026-04-23

Thanks !

Love this game...

---

B) Finkel's event card Blown Away states "Move anyone within range 2 up to 2 areas."  Does "anyone" mean any character (so, heroes and monsters), or just heroes, or some other definition I can't think of?

---
**#2** · user `1374367` · 2026-01-27 *(edited)*

[q="Chargers"]A) With cards such as Sindra's Element Staff (begins with [u]Play 6 cards[/u]) and Finkel's Rune Scroll (begins with [u]Spend 2 Practice actions[/u]), do you have to start counting after you reveal or see that quest or may you count cards or actions that you've previously done? [/q]

## Boldurs Dwarvenhelmet
*3 posts · started by krokantpudding on 2026-01-20* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3647963)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1876076` · 2026-01-20

Hi,
I do not understand the dwarvenhelmet of Boldu somehow. Why can I spend one health on the helmet to prevent one damgage when I can place the recieved damage there nonetheless? Or: Which damage am I supposed to not put on the helmet so that it makes sense to use it. I hope my question is clear, it is a bit tricky to describe 🙂 Thanks or enlightening me.

---
**#2** · user `2487` · 2026-01-20

The red number on an item is the number of times you can use that item.  You cannot "place received damage there nonetheless".

The ability of the helmet is to reduce damage you take by one.  You do that by placing a red token on the helmet.  You can use the helmet four times.  And, like all defensive items, it can be used at most once per incoming attack.

---
**#3** · user `1876076` · 2026-01-20

I thought anything that has a red number can be used to place damage there when I recieve damage. Then I got this wrong. Thanks.

---

## Ambush in the last rounds ✅
*6 posts · started by Genu1976 on 2026-01-16* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3645695)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1127492` · 2026-01-16 *(edited)*

When will the ambush happen, if the time tracker is on the last spaces (skulls)

a) immediately after moving the time tracker on this space (before rolling the monster die)

b) after roll the monster die as additional part of the Monster movement.

Thx

---
**#2** · user `250362` · 2026-01-18

I will try and answer your question. You may be using the AMBUSH term incorrectly or I am not understanding your question.

When the time tracker moves into the last series of Skull spaces the following occurs. See rules page 8 and 9.
1) If the Monster Dice is used, roll and resolve the effect. One of the effects is the [b]AMBUSH[/b] in which "[i]All heroes must place 1 new goblin adjacent to themselves. If a player stands in Grimheim, this effect is ignored for that player."[/i]
2) Monsters Move. One of the effects of Skull spaces is all monsters will [b]CHARGE[/b] and will add one additional space of movement.
3) Monsters Attack
4) Reinforcements: This does not apply to Skull spaces

---
**#3** · user `1876076` · 2026-01-19

Hi Genu,
this is something I wanted to point out in one of your Grimiheim videos in the comments. If Monsters charge, they don't do immedieatly after you roll the die, you just know then, that they will charge in their movement phase. So then you go to the regular movement phase and simply add one point of movement. Monsters can only gain one extra movement point per round, s if you roll the charge on the die and you are in one of the last three rounds, there will still be only one charge (anstürmen) 🙂
Grüße

> Correct. If you roll the charge side, all monsters are charging anyway, so the dice doesn't affect the level 1 monsters. All monsters charge.

## Alva's Singing Bow + Bracers = 2 Attack Actions?
*4 posts · started by mayimstith on 2026-01-10* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3642783)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3338198` · 2026-01-11 *(edited)*

Question about singing bow + Alva's bracers:

Does using Alva's bracers trigger the effect of the singing bow? 
In the rules it states a “free action” can never be an “attack action.” However, Alva's bracers instruct to “perform an attack action.” 
The singing bow also states that its power happens after “each attack action.” 
If used this way, it is easy to get the 3 mana requirement ( bracers+ regular attack+ mana at turn end) each turn. So, Alva can do 2 attack actions each turn, is this correct? Or is an attack action strictly only the action as marked with the red square tile?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2026-01-11

That works, yes! The rule about free actions not being attack actions is that some players think that playing a card which rolls a few dice counts as an attack, but it doesn't. However, if you are instructed to perform an attack action, that is an actual attack action.

---
**#3** · user `3338198` · 2026-01-12

Thank you so much! We love the game :)

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2026-01-12

Great to hear that :)

## Alva´s ability to deal damage "Hail of arrows"
*2 posts · started by Affe_mit_Waffe on 2026-01-04* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3638950)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4480412` · 2026-01-04

Hello,

the charakter Alva has from the start the ability "Hail of arrows".
Can the 3 damge be applied on only one monster, or must there be 3 independet targets?
What is, if there only 2 monsters?

---
**#2** · user `1032765` · 2026-01-05

[q="Affe_mit_Waffe"]Hello,

the charakter Alva has from the start the ability "Hail of arrows".
Can the 3 damge be applied on only one monster, or must there be 3 independet targets?
What is, if there only 2 monsters?
[/q]

You can only assign 1 damage to a monster. (Same in the upgraded version).

If there are only 2 (or even 1) monsters you forfeit the other damage.
So the upgraded version is a lot more efficient.

## Questions after 1st play
*4 posts · started by SolidSnake1123 on 2025-12-31* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3636742)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1256093` · 2026-01-01

Does mana regeneration accumulate during each turn on cards?  For example: Riposte (2) mana allows 2 generations per turn but if i dont use it every turn does it just keep accumulating mana?

Also Singing Bow states 10 attack need to be done in a forest.  Does that mean 10 attack actions or 10 attack dice total in a forest spot?

Do Legends count as monsters (keyword): For example kick does 1 damage to a monster and moves it away 1 spot?

Can you keep doing event cards for example multiple copies of vigilance allow 1 damage to adjacent monsters after their move step, so i could chain these one after an other on 1 monster?

Multishot says target 2 monsters within range and do a 2(Attack) against them?  Does this mean roll 2 attack dice against 2 each?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2026-01-01

Hi Kyle!

I hope you're enjoying the game!

1) Mana generation has no limit, you can have any amount of mana on a card, but it may only be used once per turn unless specified otherwise. So you can "store up" several uses.

2) Singing Bow uses the axe symbol, which is the symbol for the number of dice you throw. So it is 10 attack dice thrown in a forest. Keep track of progress with mini dice or markers, as it is almost impossible to roll all 10 in one go.

3) Yes, legends are also monsters. Several effects specifically say "non-legend monster" to differentiate them. Also, legends are above rank 3, meaning that effects referring to rank 1, 2, and 3 cannot be used on legends.

4) Yes, you can play any number of event cards in your turn, and any number of reaction cards on a monster turn. In the case of Vigilance, yes, you can play several of them to deal more damage to a monster. The only caveat is that each such card is its own effect. So if you are encountering a Draugr, which has Armor 1, each vigilance will be blocked by the armor.

5) Yes, you roll 2 dice against the first, then 2 other dice against the second. (Great way to roll many dice in a forest for getting Singing Bow).

Happy New Year!

---
**#3** · user `27282` · 2026-04-27

4) Yes, you can play any number of event cards in your turn

I read in the book , you can play one card of event
??????

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2026-04-27

You might be referring to monster events, which is limited to one per player. Those events are the promo pack events which are shuffled into the monster cards.
The event cards you hold in your hand, however, are free actions to play.

---

## What is the point of spawning in the last round
*4 posts · started by RaveKev on 2025-11-23* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3616716)

**#2** · user `453569` · 2025-11-23

pretty sure there's no spawning icon for the last round - but for the first round. Maybe you've gone the wrong direction. The track goes from the top to the bottom.

## Charging to attack
*9 posts · started by alfirst on 2025-11-14* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3611283)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `917332` · 2025-11-14

If monster is not on a straight path to a hero - but if it charges it will become adjacent (hero will be on the left or right of the monster) - does it charge by the rule (of monster will attack after charging it charges) - or only if hero is directly in front of the monster- blocking the path to the city

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-11-14

As long as moving an additional step in their path allows them to attack when they previously couldn't, they will charge.

---
**#3** · user `217414` · 2025-11-20

So they will interupt their direct route to the city to make a sidestep to charge and attack you even if this doesn't brings them closer to the city?

---
**#4** · user `917332` · 2025-11-20

No - I do not think so - my question was if you hero is not on a path - will they charge if they become adjacent;
But in the rules they say - monsters never divert from the path (unless your using the monster die)

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#5** · user `430700` · 2025-11-20

They never deviate from their paths when charging. But they may attack any hero standing adjacent to them. This means that they may charge 1 extra step (still following their path) if that places them adjacent to a hero. It doesn't matter if the hero is on the monster path or not, as long as the hero is adjacent to an area on the monster path. Hard to explain with words sometimes...

---
**#6** · user `217414` · 2025-11-21

That's true!! But it's clear to me now, Thank you! Love the game by the way 😉

---
**#7** · user `1191012` · 2026-04-05

[q="Lord_Aethan"]They never deviate from their paths when charging. But they may attack any hero standing adjacent to them. This means that they may charge 1 extra step (still following their path) if that places them adjacent to a hero. It doesn't matter if the hero is on the monster path or not, as long as the hero is adjacent to an area on the monster path. Hard to explain with words sometimes...[/q]

Good to know, we were a bit uncertain about the charging rules in our last game. Based on that, I think we played it correctly (for the most part). We were still not sure about the Fire Horde. I mean, they obviously (?) don't charge when they can already attack. But would they do their normal move if they can already attack? How I understand the rules is that monster only don't move when they are adjacent to a hero. So in Fire Horde's case, they would still move until they are adjacent (even if they could attack without moving), so their ability to do ranged combat wouldn't matter in that regard?

---
**#8** · user `2044257` · 2026-04-06

[q="Pjupe"]

Good to know, we were a bit uncertain about the charging rules in our last game. Based on that, I think we played it correctly (for the most part). We were still not sure about the Fire Horde. I mean, they obviously (?) don't charge when they can already attack.[/q]

Correct! They do not charge if they can attack without charging. 



[q="Pjupe"]

 But would they do their normal move if they can already attack? How I understand the rules is that monster only don't move when they are adjacent to a hero. So in Fire Horde's case, they would still move until they are adjacent (even if they could attack without moving), so their ability to do ranged combat wouldn't matter in that regard?[/q]

Exactly. That is the difference between moving and charging. Moving happens always (unless being adjacent to a hero or blocked by other monsters in front of them). Charging happens only if monsters cannot attack anyone after moving and the extra step (following the path to Grimheim) would allow them to attack. 

So, Fire Horde monsters do never consider if they can attack someone at range 2 or not before moving, they just move. It is after moving that they start "thinking" if they can attack or not in their current position. If they can attack, they stay where they are. If they cant attack, they consider charging to the next hex in their path. If charging allows them to attack, they charge. If charging still does not allow them to attack, they do not charge. 

You have to thing a little bit more when considering charging with Fire Horde compared to other factions, especially when Surt gives them range 3 :-). 
Just some advice, it can be dangerous to stay at Robbers Camp when Surt appears :-)

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#9** · user `430700` · 2026-04-06

Just a clarification:
The only thing that prevents Fire Horde from moving is characters blocking its path, or standing adjacent to a hero. It will move on its path, even if that causes it to no longer attack a hero. It will not "stay" within range and skip moving to attack, it will only go an _extra_ step to attack, by charging. This is a given with all range 1 monsters, because they will never be able to move away from an adjacent hero anyway, but Fire Horde may in some cases (when you're standing behind them), move out of range, leading to not attacking.

---

## Question about "War Banners" (campaign)
*2 posts · started by Laubfrosch on 2025-11-13* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3610634)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `240242` · 2025-11-13

We are not sure how to interpret the "War Banners" card in the campaign: Is the first space of the time track that technically is a reinforcement space considered to also count? Because normally you set up the game, place the monsters, but then it's the players turn first. So we tend to think that it doesn't count as a "reinforcement turn" (the term used on the card) and the monsters won't move immediately. Is our understanding correct here?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-11-14

Yes, the monsters move before the reinforcement step, so there are no monsters in play at that time.

## Ability to deal damage 
*7 posts · started by alfirst on 2025-11-11* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3609126)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `917332` · 2025-11-11

Alva ability to deal damage for spending mana I believe - can it be applied to a different monster - not the one you have attacked 
Say - you successfully attacked one with a dice roll and then want to use ability on another one? (Effectively killing both - assuming they are in the range)
Or you can only do it on the monster you are attacking?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-11-11

Each attack has 1 target. If an ability or effect adds damage to an attack, it is added to the damage against THAT target, not any other target. If an ability or effect simply deals damage separately from the attack, it can have its own target.

---
**#3** · user `917332` · 2025-11-11 *(edited)*

Card is «throwing darts”
Put a damage - to roll 3 attack on adjacent monster 

It does not say during attack action - so I can assume 
It is a stand alone ability - effectively giving 2nd attack option

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-11-14

Yes, a second way to deal damage, but only with 3 dice, and its doesn't count as an attack action, so you don't get normal attack bonuses.

---
**#5** · user `917332` · 2025-11-15

Not sure what you mean “normal attack bonuses” - gold? 
In the rules it says though - page 7 - whenever you kill a monster (directly or indirectly, through attacks or other effects) you gain experience - so looks like 
It does not matter what killed the monster

---
**#6** · user `1374367` · 2025-11-15

[q="alfirst"]Not sure what you mean “normal attack bonuses” - gold?[/q]
No. "Attack bonuses" as in effects coming from cards. If a card gives you X when attacking that wouldn't be valid as it doesn't count as an attack action.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#7** · user `430700` · 2025-11-15

Yeah, for example, if Bjorn has the ability "Long Shot II", it adds damage based on the distance to the target, but that is only valid in attack actions, not when using other effects. That's what I mean by attack bonuses.

---

## Multiple spawns in one location
*3 posts · started by DonCazino on 2025-11-06* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3606382)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1086141` · 2025-11-06

1: We had 2 spawns in the same location. It was red card spawns, so there wasn’t room for all the monsters. What would be the best way to handle that? ( we houseruled that we just drew another spawn since it would otherwise leave a legend out). 

2: When Sindra mind control a trollkin to attack another monster, would the trollkin get the bonus dice for adjencancy to other trollkin?

---
**#2** · user `1246` · 2025-11-06

[q="DonCazino"]1: We had 2 spawns in the same location. It was red card spawns, so there wasn’t room for all the monsters. What would be the best way to handle that? ( we houseruled that we just drew another spawn since it would otherwise leave a legend out). 

2: When Sindra mind control a trollkin to attack another monster, would the trollkin get the bonus dice for adjencancy to other trollkin?
[/q]

In some situations, not all monsters can be placed as indicated on the card. If so, put
the card at the bottom of the deck and draw a new one until you get a card that can be
placed.
These are some examples where you need to draw a new card:
* If there are not enough monster tiles available in the supply.
* If you draw a Legend card and that Legend tile is already in play.
* If one or more of the indicated areas are occupied.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-11-06

And for question 2, yes! The effect of the trollkin doesn't go away because she is controlling the troll. In fact, sometimes she is so convincing in her mind tricks that she gets trollkin to support their attackers :)

## Miniatures setup
*4 posts · started by Argand on 2025-11-03* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3604475)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `921866` · 2025-11-03

I have a question about the setup: When it says to place the hero figure in Grimheim, when there are 4 players there isn't enough physical space between the houses to place them. Is it allowed to place the heroes adjacent to the yellow village line?
It's a big difference; in one case the first action might involve moving out of the village, in the other it could be anything else.
Thanks

---
**#2** · user `36112` · 2025-11-03

Dunno if this helps, but, remember all of Grimheim is considered to be One Big Space on the board.

---
**#3** · user `364816` · 2025-11-03

[q="LemonyFresh"]Dunno if this helps, but, remember all of Grimheim is considered to be One Big Space on the board.[/q]
This. In other words, just cram the buildings and miniatures together in Grimheim, it doesn't matter which is put where, and it doesn't matter if there is more than one thing on a hex.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-11-05

Grimheim is very crammed when you're playing with 4 heroes, and sometimes you need to adjust their physical placement for the initial startup. But it doesn't have any rules significance. All heroes are in Grimheim, even if their footstands extend a bit beyond the border. Generally, this is only happening on the very first turn and then never again during the same game.

**#2** · user `3794671` · 2025-11-02

Both cards. You always have to discard an event card to perform its effect.

## Sindras Chain Reaction and Meditation
*3 posts · started by Nomisis on 2025-10-11* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3590887)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4386046` · 2025-10-11 *(edited)*

Hey everyone, 

love the game, played a few rounds, still learning the rules since there are new questions coming up every match. Having lots of fun though.

Many question have been answered going through many threads here, thanks to the Fryxelius family's activity here. I appreciate that a lot.

4 things coming to my mind anyway.

1. When exiting the Naglfar, do I have to walk over the tile where the road goes, or can I take a shortcut to the northwestern tiles, that are connected but do not have direct road link?

2. To finish a quest for an equipment card that demands it, can I do an attack in an area without any monsters in it? Otherwise that quest might be impossible since monsters may never appear there.

3. Sindras Chain reaction attacks 3 monsters. Does it have to be 3 different monsters or can the first and the 3rd be on the same one (for example because only 2 monsters are in range)? It would then technically still be a chain reaction, but I think that is not how the card was meant.

4. Sindras Meditation II.
Does it mean I can freely move mana around at any time, or at any time in my turn, or once per turn when I basically "use this ability"?
This can be extremely important in combination with the defensive crystal that she can find as an equipment. In the endgame this one can make her almost invulnerable with a total mana generation of possibly 8+ per turn.

---
**#2** · user `1374367` · 2025-10-12 *(edited)*

[q="Nomisis"]1. When exiting the Naglfar, do I have to walk over the tile where the road goes, or can I take a shortcut to the northwestern tiles, that are connected but do not have direct road link? [/q]
You don't have to follow the road.

[q="Nomisis"]2. To finish a quest for an equipment card that demands it, can I do an attack in an area without any monsters in it? Otherwise that quest might be impossible since monsters may never appear there. [/q]
[-]You don't have a target in range and can therefore not make an attack.[/-] I misunderstood the question.

3-4: What's the text on the cards?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-10-12

1. Any side, but not into a water area.
2. If a quest tells you to "spend an attack action", it means you forfeit the action (move the action marker there but do not attack, you are doing the quest instead of the normal effect). So you do not need any adjacent monsters to "spend an attack action". In fact, it is better if you don't.
3. No, it targets 3 monsters. 
4. At all times, it is a passive effect.
Cheers!

## Monster movement - stuck "conga line" ✅
*5 posts · started by Ed_Sanches on 2025-09-28* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3583854)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4373808` · 2025-09-28

I just picked up the game this weekend and we had a blast. It feels like you are playing Dungeons and Dragons. And we are long time fans of Castle Panic !
My only issue with the game is monster movement. Since we were playing with 4 players, we basically stationed outside Grimheim in a square-shape formation and basically stopped all the monsters from moving and they just stacked behind the other monsters like a conga-line. 
We did use the monster die, which I know has the maneuver option. But even then it felt like the monsters were just hanging there. 
Is there any way to make them deviate from the path and go around the players and reach Grimheim?
I know this will make the game considerably more challenging, but it makes sense.

---
**#2** · user `364816` · 2025-09-29

That's actually the most interesting part of the game in terms of strategy, and I think it's impossible to win at higher difficulty levels without abusing these positioning rules. So, the rules as written don't allow you to change that, no.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430994` · 2025-09-29

> ↳ *Replying to #2 (user `364816`):* That's actually the most interesting part of the game in terms of strategy, and I think it's impossible to win at higher difficulty levels without abusing these positioning rules. So, the rules as written don't allow you…

> It is a very important feature for the game since there is usually not enough time to kill all monsters. But stopping them like this from several directions also put your heroes at risk of being knocked out.
> Maybe you had lucky monster spawns (it happens) where they mostly come from one side, or mostly small monsters. A bunch of imps or sprites may not be the most dangerous lategame, but face 2 layers of Elementals and Jotunn, and you will feel the pain.
> 4 of the 6 sides on the monster dice are dangerous in your scenario: Extra attack strength can mean you die. Moving clockwise/anti-clockwise often means more monsters can reach you or even that they 'dance' into town. And the push side can move you back into town if you stand just outside, allowing the monsters to rush in. Remember, the monsters make their move just after the monster dice
>
> You do have a point of course, and that is one of the main reasons for the limit of max 4 players - with more, it becomes too easy to block all sides, reducing strategy.
>
> Cheers!

## Eitri's Pick Question
*8 posts · started by Sprogz on 2025-09-21* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3579818)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2231395` · 2025-09-21 *(edited)*

Eitri's Pick quest states [q][u]End your movement adjacent to 4 monsters or 1 legend[/u] to pick a fight..[/q]

If during the Monster Turn 4 monsters end up adjacent a Boldur, and assuming Boldur survives the Monster Attack phase, can he pick up Eitri's Pick at the start of his turn as he is adjacent to 4 monsters and it's not exactly clear what "End your movement" actually means.

---
**#2** · user `1374367` · 2025-09-21 *(edited)*

[q="Sprogz"]Eitri's Pick quest states [q][u]End your movement adjacent to 4 monsters or 1 legend[/u] to pick a fight..[/q]

If during the Monster Turn 4 monsters end up adjacent a Boldur, and assuming Boldur survives the Monster Attack phase, can he pick up Eitri's Pick at the start of his turn as he is adjacent to 4 monsters and it's not exactly clear what "End your movement" actually means.[/q]
No. For you to be able to pick a fight you'll have to first spend one move action in order to "End your movement" adjacent to monsters/legend. Edit: However, you may move 0 areas.

---
**#3** · user `2231395` · 2025-09-21 *(edited)*

Thanks. The act of having to spend something to pick up the equipment makes sense.

The text on the card however doesn't state Move [b]Action[/b], just "End your [i]movement[/i]," so how about playing Maneuver (Move 1 area) or Seek Shelter (Move up to 2 areas into a [i]location[/i] first? Both those cards are definitely [i]movement[/i].

---
**#4** · user `1374367` · 2025-09-21

[q="Sprogz"]The text on the card however doesn't state Move [b]Action[/b], just "End your [i]movement[/i]," so how about playing Maneuver (Move 1 area) or Seek Shelter (Move up to 2 areas into a [i]location[/i] first? Both those cards are definitely [i]movement[/i].[/q]
I've read it as meaning the movement to be in reference to an action. You have a valid point. I hope Fryxelius can clarify it for us.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#5** · user `430700` · 2025-09-21

No action is needed per se, any movement would do.

---
**#6** · user `2231395` · 2025-09-21 *(edited)*

[q="Lord_Aethan"]No action is needed per se, any movement would do.[/q]

Thank you. 

Even if, as @Tronin suggested, it's a Move Action where you stay put and choose not to move at all?

I guess I'm trying to get to the point of whether it's the actual [b]act[/b] of moving [i][b]one[/b] or more[/i] areas (so 0 areas doesn't count) or the act of spending some action or card that is [i]movement[/i] even if you don't actually move.

---
**#7** · user `1374367` · 2025-09-21 *(edited)*

[q="Sprogz"]Even if, as @Tronin suggested, it's a Move Action where you stay put and choose not to move at all?

I guess I'm trying to get to the point of whether it's the actual [b]act[/b] of moving [i][b]one[/b] or more[/i] areas (so 0 areas doesn't count) or the act of spending some action or card that is [i]movement[/i] even if you don't actually move.[/q]
If we look at the Move Action as an example the rules says: "Move - Move your hero up to 3 areas on the board." The writing suggests you move 0-3 areas. You will then fulfill the requirement for the quest "Eitri's Pick" as you have ended your movement, even though you never moved.

"Maneuver" that tells you to move 1 area will not be able to fulfill the requirement as the card requires you to move 1 area. "Seek Shelter" on the other hand will, as it tells you to move 0-2 areas for a successful movement.

---
**#8** · user `2231395` · 2025-09-21

Thanks. Yes, that makes perfect sense. 👍

---

## Do multiple Event cards stack?  ✅
*5 posts · started by hexfeld on 2025-09-15* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3576633)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2067408` · 2025-09-15

I guess the answer is yes, but just to be sure: can I play multiple cards for their bonuses on the same action? For example two cards that add 4 dice each to the attack roll.

---
**#2** · user `364816` · 2025-09-15

I don't see anything in the rules that prevent this, so I'd say yes! At least, that's how I play.

---
**#3** · user `2067408` · 2025-09-15

Thanks. For Alva, this makes her getting the bow for rolling 10 dice much easier....

> [q="hexfeld"]Thanks. For Alva, this makes her getting the bow for rolling 10 dice much easier.... [/q]
> The quest doesn't require you to roll 10 dice in a single roll, just 10 dice total. It can be spread out over several turns.

[q="Fryxen"][q="hexfeld"]Thanks. For Alva, this makes her getting the bow for rolling 10 dice much easier.... [/q]
The quest doesn't require you to roll 10 dice in a single roll, just 10 dice total. It can be spread out over several turns.
Cheers![/q]
Yes, but due to some luck I had 2 +4 dice cards. So it was easy to get the bow in just one turn. That said, I haven't won one game on hard. I lose constantly 3 or 4 rounds before game end.... 

Thank you for being so active here on bgg! I love this game!

## Blinding flash + Deja vu
*5 posts · started by ElusiveAuroraGlacier on 2025-09-03* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3570491)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4285206` · 2025-09-03

Can you use blinding flash with deja vu?

Or does the monster attack happening outside your turn (during monster attack phase) mean you cannot combine them?

Blinding flash: Play before a monster attacks you. Ignore the attack.

Deja Vu: Once per turn, when playing a card, perform its effect twice.

---
**#2** · user `1374367` · 2025-09-03

[q="ElusiveAuroraGlacier"]Can you use blinding flash with deja vu?

Or does the monster attack happening outside your turn (during monster attack phase) mean you cannot combine them?

Blinding flash: Play before a monster attacks you. Ignore the attack.

Deja Vu: Once per turn, when playing a card, perform its effect twice.[/q]
The monster attack happens outside of your turn, so no.

---
**#3** · user `3224330` · 2025-09-03 *(edited)*

And even if it did work there wouldn't be two attacks to ignore during the point where blinding flash is played.  Deja Vu does not let you perform a card's effect, delay, and then perform the effect again.  It's gotta be twice in a row immediately.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-09-04

The "turn" referenced by Deja Vu is your own turn, not every player turn or monster turn.

**#5** · user `72225` · 2025-10-29

This should be in the rules forum

## Direction Arrows on board
*9 posts · started by dcrystal on 2025-08-14* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3559364)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-14

1) why are there direction arrows outside spawn locations?
2) what arrows govern for monster movent?  I've been playing it that spawn location arrows govern but now am facing spawns outside the red areas and suspect that may not be true?
3) when a monster is on a hex that has multiple "close" arrows..and either can apply am i 'required' to change directions if it will get them around a blockade or is this player choice?

---
**#2** · user `1374367` · 2025-08-14

A monster will follow the direction of the arrow behind him towards Grimheim until he gets to a road. When on a road the monster will follow it to Grimheim.

---
**#3** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-15 *(edited)*

yes...  i get that.. but what do i do when the monster is equal distance from 2 direction arrows and isn't on a road?..     either direction would take him to a road.  

also when 1 direction is blocked by another non-moving monster.. does the one behind just site there (when it has the option to chose from 2 direction arrows "behind him"..) or am i forced to change his path to bypass the blockage?

[imageid=9046927 inline]

the skeleton (house added for clarity).. does he move or stay put?  he's equal distance to 2 directions behind him.. both lead to a road that would take him to Grim.

and if he does move, do i keep him on that direction for the next turn.. or can he change again (if not beside a player).

---
**#4** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-15

Extra Q.

Queen of the dead spawn on nailfare (sp?)..  and it has no arrows.. does she just sit there waiting for me?

---
**#5** · user `364816` · 2025-08-15

There are arrows corresponding to non-spawn locations because it is possible to move monsters away from their hexes, so they may end up in rows that no longer correspond to spawn locations.

As to your example with the skeleton on the house, it tries to go further south-east, which will be blocked, so it won't move.

---
**#6** · user `1374367` · 2025-08-15

[q="Trantor42"]As to your example with the skeleton on the house, it tries to go further south-east, which will be blocked, so it won't move.[/q]
Correct.

Again: A monster will follow the direction of the arrow behind him towards Grimheim until he gets to a road. [b]All other arrows are irrelevant.[/b] So the arrow on the other side of the road will never affect him.

---

## Movement question 
*2 posts · started by NormandoAraujo on 2025-08-13* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3558482)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3145643` · 2025-08-13

Guys could you please verify if my retional is correct ?

According to the rules shown, a monster never makes two charges in the same turn.
A “charge” is simply a +1 area movement bonus, and the rule clearly states “will never take more than 1 additional step”.
So, even if two conditions trigger a charge (for example, the skull event and also being one step away from attacking a hero), the monster still gains only one extra step in total.

---
**#2** · user `364816` · 2025-08-13

Correct.

---

## 1 monster and 2 players..
*7 posts · started by dcrystal on 2025-08-13* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3558366)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-13

if a monster is adjacent to 2 players how is it's target chosen?

is there a hierarchy (least health left, most total HP, strongest (for dice) etc) or is it just player choice?

---
**#2** · user `364816` · 2025-08-13

Player's choice.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-08-13

Yes, player choice. This is actually one of the more important aspects of the cooperation in the game, standing where you can take some of the hits another player would otherwise take. Especially with the fire horde that have attack range 2. They are not as strong as other monsters, but their range means you will likely get attacked by a lot of them. So splitting those attacks between 2 players is sometimes the only way to survive.

For the red monster version of Grendel, who attacks twice, this is also important, because getting hit twice by him could kill any hero, even from 0 damage. So to be safe, you either need a lot of protective equipment, protection events, or you need to split his 2 attacks between 2 defender heroes.

---
**#4** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-13

[q="Lord_Aethan"]For the red monster version of Grendel, who attacks twice, this is also important, because getting hit twice by him could kill any hero, even from 0 damage. So to be safe, you either need a lot of protective equipment, protection events, or you need to split his 2 attacks between 2 defender heroes.[/q]

getting hit once by a troll can kill any player from 0 damage.. lol.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#5** · user `430700` · 2025-08-13

Only if he is boosted by other trollkin, or if you are playing Boldur. The troll has 6 dice so if you are undamaged, you will not die from one hit.

---
**#6** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-13

[q="Lord_Aethan"]Only if he is boosted by other trollkin, or if you are playing Boldur. The troll has 6 dice so if you are undamaged, you will not die from one hit.[/q]
i've never been that lucky when it comes to their dice rolls.  troll 6+3 all hits on my wizard guy (9hp).

---
**#7** · user `4373808` · 2025-09-29

well, if you are a wizard facing a 9-die troll by yourself, you are begging to be smashed ! 💀

## Troll cave..
*3 posts · started by dcrystal on 2025-08-12* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3558363)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-13 *(edited)*

2 Qs.

1) do you "have" to enter the cave from 1 of the 2 hex sides on the road.. or can you get in from any adjacent hex?
2) when in the cave "area" can you still attack and be attacked by things outside it?..  or is it isolated?

---
**#2** · user `1374367` · 2025-08-13

[q="dcrystal"]2 Qs.

1) do you "have" to enter the cave from 1 of the 2 hex sides on the road.. or can you get in from any adjacent hex?
2) when in the cave "area" can you still attack and be attacked by things outside it?..  or is it isolated?[/q]
1. You don't have to follow the road and can enter from any adjacent area. However, I don't believe you have to enter the area containing the name specifically as all 3 areas are inside the yellow boarder making them all part of the same location.

2. Attacks can still happen.

---
**#3** · user `364816` · 2025-08-13

1) From any adjacent hex.
2) Everything works as normal. Don't try to think of it as a cave that allows you shelter. It's just a hex with a special name that may come up on certain quests or events, but for all other gameplay purposes, it works like any other hex.

## Monster movement
*2 posts · started by dcrystal on 2025-08-12* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3558354)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-13

They won't move if adjacent to a player.. ok.

so if a monster (goblin) has move 2, and both move 1 & 2 would put them adjacent to a player (or even the same one) does movement stop or do they go max?

---
**#2** · user `1374367` · 2025-08-13

[q="dcrystal"]They won't move if adjacent to a player.. ok.

so if a monster (goblin) has move 2, and both move 1 & 2 would put them adjacent to a player (or even the same one) does movement stop or do they go max?[/q]
They would stop as soon as they are adjacent to a player and forfeit any remaining steps.

## Timing of Attack Rolls and abilities and more questions.
*4 posts · started by Coco_Games on 2025-08-10* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3556712)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3343009` · 2025-08-10

Hey we have the German Version and I am wondering when to use certain cards. For example with Björns ability I am pretty Sure that you can spand the Focus Action for additional damage AFTER the roll. With cards that add more sice to the roll I am pretty Sure you have to so it BEFORE rolling the dice.

However for example Alvas Flexibility Just say to add 2 damage to an Attack. Would I have to decide this AFTER or BEFORE the dice roll?

Also  5 more questions:

- Can I use multiple Events to modify a single Action (e.q. Play the Alva Card that adds 4 dice to a roll twice for +8 dice?)

- Alvas Flexibility Says to add +1 range for the Turn. That probably means of you do multiple range dependent Things in a Turn that improves all of them?

- The witch spawned skeletons around the temple Ruins and for those Not on a path we were a bit unsere about movement direction.

- Can you enter/Exit grimheim with tiny Bonus movement actions (That Björn Equipment for example?)

- Draugr Block 1 from all sources of damage and Not Just Attack Rolls right? For example Alva's starting ability ist useless against them right?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-08-10

Hi! 

Generally, you may always add and modify attack results AFTER rolling the dice, unless the effect says otherwise.

As for the other questions: 
1) Yes, you may use multiple events or effects to modify your attack results.
2) Yes, many of the effects of Alva and Bjorn depend on their attack range, and this adds range for the whole turn.
3) Draw invisible lines from all the arrows at the edge of the board to the roads. That's their paths. In this case, they all want to go to the road, so in reality, only a few of them will move and then block the movement of everyone else. 
4) Yes! That is often the most effective way, not having to spend a whole action on it.
5) That's right, Hail of Arrows is useless against draugr.
5)

---
**#3** · user `3343009` · 2025-08-10 *(edited)*

Thanks for the reply and Help. Just to make Sure. If I want to add dice (and not damage) to a roll I have to play that Card/Ability before rolling right?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-08-11

No, you can add them after rolling, just roll more dice. As long as it doesn't specifically say to play the cards before rolling, you may add dice and damage after the roll.

---

## Embla's cards for moving and automatic kill ?
*5 posts · started by Mormorod on 2025-08-08* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3555667)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `438279` · 2025-08-08

Embla has several abilities that allow her to move 1 space.
She also has the ability to kill a small enemy (rank 1) at the end of her movement (Passive effect).

If she uses her movement (4 squares) and kills an little enemy (Passive Ability card), then uses another ability card to move into one region, can she kill another enemy adjacent in her new location?

(Sorry, I don't have the cards in front of me to give you the exact names.)

---
**#2** · user `1374367` · 2025-08-08

[q="Mormorod"]Embla has several abilities that allow her to move 1 space.
She also has the ability to kill a small enemy (rank 1) at the end of her movement (Passive effect).

If she uses her movement (4 squares) and kills an little enemy (Passive Ability card), then uses another ability card to move into one region, can she kill another enemy adjacent in her new location?

(Sorry, I don't have the cards in front of me to give you the exact names.)
[/q]
No. "Your ability cards may only be used [b]once per turn[/b] (except cards that prevent damage – they may be used once each time you receive damage)."

---
**#3** · user `438279` · 2025-08-08

Oh ! Of course 👌

Thanks !

---
**#4** · user `3644172` · 2025-08-08

And the ability that allows you to kill a small enemy works after a movement action. The different abilities that allow her to move 1 space are not movement actions.

---
**#5** · user `3224330` · 2025-08-09

[q="Biky_One"]And the ability that allows you to kill a small enemy works after a movement action. The different abilities that allow her to move 1 space are not movement actions.[/q]

This more than the other response.  Because I believe that Embla's card states that it can be used with each movement action.  So as a passive effect it can be used more than once per turn.  But much like free actions that give you attacks, free actions that give you movement do not count as movement actions.  So I'm not aware of any way for her to get more than one movement action per turn.

[q="Ynsa"]It sounds to me that Deju vu is kinda overpowered if you can use the ability on every player turn and monster turn alike. For instance conaider the following:

🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-07-29

The card is intended to be used on his turn only. It says "once per turn", and it implicitly means each of _your_ turns. Unfortunately, it is a bit ambiguous and should be improved in future prints. But no, you may only use this effect on Finkel's turn.
(For full disclosure, I think I might have answered otherwise in another thread, but I did not think through the consequences of allowing that).

## Attacking into or out of Grimheim
*11 posts · started by Cargilflo on 2025-07-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3546223)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3522744` · 2025-07-22

If I'm in Grinheim, can a monster attack me? And can I attack? Thanks.

---
**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-07-22

No, as per the rules.

---
**#3** · user `1898967` · 2025-08-15

So if I am in Grimheim I don't block enemy movement and the "just walk into it"?

---
**#4** · user `1374367` · 2025-08-15

[q="Brezel85"]So if I am in Grimheim I don't block enemy movement and the "just walk into it"?[/q]
Correct.

---
**#5** · user `1898967` · 2025-08-15

But this only is true for Grimheim? I am not save from being attacked in other locations, right?

---
**#6** · user `1374367` · 2025-08-15

[q="Brezel85"]But this only is true for Grimheim? I am not save from being attacked in other locations, right?[/q]
You are the last line of defense against the monsters. If you're not standing between the monsters and Grimheim they will march right into town and burn it to the ground (or at least one building at a time, they are quite polite).

This is only true while you're in Grimheim. Outside of town you'll stop monster movement if you can position your heroes between the monsters and Grimheim.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#7** · user `430700` · 2025-08-15

The theme is that there are some defenders among the local villagers. So when a monster enters, the locals bandage to stop and kill that monster before he could burn down more than 1 building. You - on the other hand - are hiding inside a house..

---
**#8** · user `3285410` · 2025-08-28

Dans grimheim peut ton utiliser des cartes évenements contre des monstres ? 
Comme tatane , bowling etc ...

---
**#9** · user `233443` · 2025-08-29 *(edited)*

[q="Tronin"]Outside of town you'll stop monster movement if you can position your heroes between the monsters and Grimheim.[/q]
Technically, you don't need to be "between". You can position yourself "behind" the monsters as well - as long as you keep them locked in battle with you, the monsters won't move towards Grimheim.

---
**#10** · user `1898967` · 2025-08-29

And accidentally moving onto / through mountain spaces.

**#11** · user `2231395` · 2025-09-20

[q="jonnel"][q="Tronin"]Outside of town you'll stop monster movement if you can position your heroes between the monsters and Grimheim.[/q]
Technically, you don't need to be "between". You can position yourself "behind" the monsters as well - as long as you keep them locked in battle with you, the monsters won't move towards Grimheim.[/q]

## 2 newbie questions on Abilities  ✅
*7 posts · started by Rocky123 on 2025-07-13* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3541771)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `194423` · 2025-07-13

When an ability allows you to add damage to each monster adjacent to the one you did damage or killed.. does that include adjacent if out of range of your hero… ?  Or ignore range and just do clock wise

Abilities can only be used once per turn.. except permanent adds to health or attack.. etc… but example.. elven blade says “After each attack”. So if I make my normal attack.. it triggers… but then I use another ability that lets me attack again… will her blade trigger again?

Same as Sweeping strike for Boldur

Thanks

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430994` · 2025-07-14

> ↳ *Replying to #1 (user `194423`):* When an ability allows you to add damage to each monster adjacent to the one you did damage or killed.. does that include adjacent if out of range of your hero… ? Or ignore range and just do clock wise Abilities can only…

> [q="Rocky123"]When an ability allows you to add damage to each monster adjacent to the one you did damage or killed.. does that include adjacent if out of range of your hero… ?  Or ignore range and just do clock wise
>
> Abilities can only be used once per turn.. except permanent adds to health or attack.. etc… but example.. elven blade says “After each attack”. So if I make my normal attack.. it triggers… but then I use another ability that lets me attack again… will her blade trigger again?
>
> Same as Sweeping strike for Boldur
>
> Thanks [/q]
> Only the main attack is dependent on range, not other effects unless they state a range. Boldur's Sweeping Strike hits enemies adjacent to HIM in clockwise order, not clockwise around the monster he attacks.
> Note that playing an event  that attacks a monster is not an 'attack action'. The attack action is only through your main attack and through a few cards that clearly state that they give you another attack action. Strength buffs and effects like Elven Blade are only relevant for attack actions, not whenever you roll dice or deal damage.
> There are 4 types of effects:
> - Altering your rules (Embla moves 4 instead of 3, Boldur's armor...)
> - Buffs (mostly weapons) apply to each attack action.
> - Battle effects (for example Shield that prevents wounds) can be used once in each attack, so both in your attack actions and in each case when a monster attacks you.
> - Other effects can be used once per turn.

---
**#3** · user `1634582` · 2025-07-14

Uh oh, does this mean Embla's "Move 4" means it is "Move 4 instead of the normal 3 for a move action" and NOT an extra free move? 😭 Whoops!

## Event cards promo pack
*6 posts · started by pandaone on 2025-07-04* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3537034)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3018014` · 2025-07-04

Do event cards have to be resolved when setting up the game?

---
**#2** · user `250362` · 2025-07-04

Event cards are not resolved during game set up. When setting up the game, each player shuffles their Event deck and draws one card from the top of the deck into their hand. Event cards are resolved when a player uses them during their turn.

---
**#3** · user `3018014` · 2025-07-04

I wanted to talk about the cards in promo pack 2. Sorry for the confusion

Perhaps change the thread title to something like Event Cards Promo Pack.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#5** · user `430700` · 2025-07-07

I am sorry that there is no official rule about how to handle events in setup. A lot of events are not applicable in setup, so I say you simply ignore all events in the first reinforcements. That's the easiest solution.

## Embla Card wrong translation?
*8 posts · started by Sursulapitschi on 2025-06-24* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3532448)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3673920` · 2025-06-24

Hello,
we are a bit confused:
Embla ability-card "Flotter Angriff" says in german: "Discard [b]a other[/b] card from your hand, to perform a attac action." This is absolutley overpowerd, because this text means, you could keep "Flotter Angriff" in your hand and discard in every following turn a other card to perform a attac, using "Flotter Angriff" over and over again. Should the card say: "Discard [b]a additional[/b] card from your hand..." ? So you would have to discard "Flotter Angriff" and a additional card?

---
**#2** · user `1634582` · 2025-06-25 *(edited)*

Hello, fellow defender of Grimheim!  I think you are referring to the card which, in English, is called "Speedy Attack."  If so, that is not an Ability card but, rather, an Event card. To use/activate an Event card you place it in your discard pile.  

Adding text as you suggest may have been helpful, though. :)

---
**#3** · user `3673920` · 2025-06-25

Yes, it is an Event Card. But it says discard a other card (not another card). In German that term did exclude the card, which says it. So we thought, this event will stay on your hand and you only discard a other card. So you say, it is discard both. The Speedy Attack and another card? Which would make much more sense. Many thanks, so Embla would get a downgrade :-)

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-07-02

The rules is that you discard an event card to carry out its effect. So you discard Speedy Attack to do what it says, and it says to discard another card to perform an attack action. You never perform the effect of an event card without discarding it.

So, you discard Speedy Attack to do what it says. It says you should discard another card, so you do that too. Then you may perform an attack action. This is not an error. The reason for the English reading is to make sure the player doesn't think he/she can discard the card Speedy Attack to carry out the attack action, you need to discard it along with another card.

---
**#5** · user `3673920` · 2025-07-02

Thanks Jopnathan for explaining. We play it now the right way. But the german card did not say another, it say a other (the first means one more thing, the second means a other thing, not this). In german another is not equal a other - that are different things.

---
**#6** · user `1898967` · 2025-08-16

Ja aber mag nicht perfekt übersetzt sein, das stimmt.

Aber lässt trotzdem keinen Interpretationsspielraum. Denn um die Karte auszuführen musst du sie auf deinen Ablagestapel spielen. Dann ist sie weg.

Ideal wäre vermutlich gewesen:

"Wirf eine zusätzliche Karte ab"

---
**#7** · user `3673920` · 2025-08-17

**#8** · user `1898967` · 2025-08-17

Es gibt keine Möglichkeit die Karte zu triggern und diese dann wieder auf die Hand nehmen zu dürfen. Denn das müsste dann explizit auf der Karte stehen.

## Help me
*9 posts · started by Verdan99 on 2025-06-23* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3531926)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4144645` · 2025-06-24

1 - If I'm inside the city of "Greimhein", can I attack the monsters?

2 - In the yellow areas, where there are resources to collect, can you get in anywhere inside the yellow line or do you need to go to the tile where the resources are? 

3 - Within the bodur card which says "Add a damage to each attack", each time I use an attack action I put 1 red stone on the card and when I collect some will they be the skill's damage?

---
**#2** · user `1634582` · 2025-06-24 *(edited)*

Greetings to Washington from Washington! 😛 (I live in Washington in the U.S.A.). 🙂

[b]1) Can you attack monsters whilst in Grimheim?[/b]  
No.  

([i]Rulebook Pg. 3: "Grimheim" - 1st Paragraph[/i])

2)[b] Do you have to go to the specific tile the starting/set-up resources are at or can you collect them whilst in that location/region?  [/b]  
You must go to the specific area (hex) they are at.  

([i]Rulebook Pg. 5: Game Set-up: 3A - A hero may remove them from the 'specified area.'  NOTE: However, there are some quests that may be fulfilled by being in any area within a location/region, such as Bjorn needing to spend a Mend Action in Nailfaire (Pg 7: First example) [/i]).

3)[b] How does Boldur's alternative main weapon, "Smiterbiter," work? [/b]
When you kill a monster and deal extra damage, you add the number of that surplus onto your card up to a maximum of 3, and can draw from that pool to strengthen future attacks. (e.g. (For example) You kill a 2-damage monster by dealing 4 damage, you'd place two tokens on your card, which you can use to add extra damage to a later attack).
  
([i]Rulebook Pg. 12: Abilities[/i])

Hope that helps, hope you enjoy the game, and hope you have a great evening! :)

---
**#3** · user `4144645` · 2025-06-24

The card says: add one damage to each attack action.


Each time I attack I put a stone on the card, is each stone a damage point for this skill? For example, if I attack 10 times, will this skill cause damage level 10 when used?

I have really enjoyed your game, I'm playing a lot, and I'm looking for the next expansions.

---
**#4** · user `1634582` · 2025-06-24

Ah; are you referring to Boldur's ability card "Sweeping Strike?"  
I was confused by your comment about adding a stone.  If the card in question is "Sweeping Strike," no stone is necessary.  You simply get +1 damage for each attack action (Powerful!!! 🙂).  Then, assuming that monster was an adjacent one, and is killed, if there is damage left over you could apply that amount of damage to the second monster.  

If I haven't addressed the correct card (Sweeping Strike or Smiterbiter (see the reply above)), let me know; perhaps I missed one that may apply. 

Thank you, so much, for enjoying [i]my[/i] game! (Dear Fryxelius brothers: When can I expect my first check to arrive??? 😛 hehe).  It's not my game, but I am glad to help, and glad that you're enjoying their game, too! 😛

---
**#5** · user `4144645` · 2025-06-24

Can you give me an example? I don't understand "You simply get +1 damage [i]for each attack action[/i]" I have 1 or 2 attack action for turn only

---
**#6** · user `1634582` · 2025-06-24

Each of those attacks you'll roll, as normal, but add a bonus damage to it.  

e.g. If you roll 10 dice and score 3 points of damage, you'll take the 3 you rolled, plus add 1 (you may think of it as an 'auto-damage' because of the card) for a total of 4 damage.  Then, if you attack again, even on the same turn, and get 8 damage on a roll, you would add +1 damage due to the card, for a total of 9 damage.

## Bjorn - Nailed Together, range?
*4 posts · started by ElusiveAuroraGlacier on 2025-06-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3531129)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4285206` · 2025-06-22

Adjacent and further away, does this mean unlimited range?

Is the area of effect a cone behind or only the exact 1 hexline behind the target in the direction Bjorn attacked the monster?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-06-23

This effect can create quite the trickshots. It basically has unlimited range, you just need to reach the first monster, then the arrow just goes on and on.
Each step must be adjacent to the previous one, and further away from you than the previous one. It may be hard to visualize in text, but those are the simple conditions. If you wonder whether the arrow can go to a specific monster, just count how far away it is, check that it is adjacent to the first monster and 1 step farther away and you're good :)

---
**#3** · user `3644172` · 2025-06-24

So it has not to be a straight line from Bjorn?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-07-02

No. Let's say you start shooting in a certain direction in a straight line, and you hit your target, dealing 5 damage more than it could take. There are 3 possible areas the arrow can continue to, which are all adjacent to the monster and also farther away from Bjorn. One directly behind, but also one to the left and one to the right. All those 3 areas are actually farther away and adjacent. He can twist the shot in any direction he wants. Let's say he chooses to spin the arrow to the right and hit a monster there which can only take 2 damage, leaving 3 damage to be dealt to a third monster. Now the arrow has only 2 possible routes, because all other areas are closer, or equally close to Bjorn as the monster you just killed.

Even though it might be a bit hard to visualize, especially in words alone, the rules are very simple. The arrow can continue 1 area, if that area is farther away from Bjorn than the previous target.

---

## Sindra - Bowling - Where is directly behind, and where may the monsters be moved?
*2 posts · started by ElusiveAuroraGlacier on 2025-06-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3531125)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4285206` · 2025-06-22

1. In what direction is directly behind? Is it in the direction you perform the action as per where your hero stands? Or does it pertain to the field itself and behind is further towards the edge of the field?

2. "may be moved 1 area" is this only in the direction of the bowling ball or can you move them 1 area in any direction? 
If for instance this is the field [S,M1,M2] and Sindra kills M1 with the ball but not M2, could you move M2 towards Sindra as the slot M1 occupied is now vacant?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-06-23

1) You target an adjacent monster, so that creates a line from you to that monster, with an area directly behind that monster, seen from your hero. Think of a straight line going from your hero, through the monster, and 1 area ahead. That's directly behind the monster.

2) This can be any direction, so in your scenario, yes, you could kill M1 and move M2 into the area where M1 just was.

---

## Boldur - Seek Shelter + Maneuver
*2 posts · started by ElusiveAuroraGlacier on 2025-06-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3531103)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4285206` · 2025-06-22 *(edited)*

1. Can Boldur use these to move onto a mountain hex?

2. Can Boldur use Seek Shelter to move into Grimheim and then out again on the other side with just this card?

3.  Seek Shelter says specifically to move into a "location". Does that mean you can only use it to move into NAMED hexes? so Witch cabin and Robber camp etc but not any other normal hex?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-06-23

1) No, you may only ever enter mountain areas if an effect specifically says so.
2) No, once you enter Grimheim, your movement ends, and the card says you cannot move more that turn.
3) Yes, locations are named areas, such as Grimheim, Robber Camp, Wyrm Lair, or Highlands. If a location contains several areas, you may use this card to refer to any area within a that location. You could - for instace - already stand in Highlands and use this card to move a couple of areas into another area also inside Highlands. The only important thing is that the target area you are moving to is a location.

---

## Boldur - Wrecking Ball & Embla -  Queen of the Hill - Move into mountains?
*2 posts · started by ElusiveAuroraGlacier on 2025-06-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3531102)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4285206` · 2025-06-22 *(edited)*

1. Wrecking Ball - "Boldur may move into occupied areas" (to attack a monster and move it 1 area)

Does this mean that Boldur can move into mountains with this card which heroes typically cannot do?

2. And how does this apply to Emblas Queen of the Hill?

3. I assume any other moves such as manouver, blown away, cane, twister etc can not put you into mountains.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-06-22

The rule that you cannot move into mountains still apply, so neither Wrecking Ball nor Queen of the Hill may be used against monsters in mountain areas.
There are only a select few effects that allow moving into mountains, and they say so specifically.

## Boldur - Sweeping strike. Attack Range & Multiple targets
*2 posts · started by ElusiveAuroraGlacier on 2025-06-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3531101)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4285206` · 2025-06-22

Sweeping Strike - "If an adjacent monster is killed in your attack action, any remaining damage may be dealt to a second monster in clockwise order"

1. The attack range isn't specified, we assume it means to a second monster in clockwise order in attack range, so the first other monster in clockwise order on any hex adjacent to Baldur. Is this correct?

2. If Baldur kills a monster and has 4 extra damage over, 3 damage kills the next target clockwise, does it also transfer to the next target clockwise and deal the remaining 1 damage to that one as well? So a total of 3 enemies hit.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-06-22

Hi! Boldur is the center of the "clock", so he sweeps around himself, going clockwise around himself. However, he may only hit a maximum of 2 enemies with this effect, any excess damage after that is wasted. (We actually did have an unlimited version in betatesting, but it was simply too powerful.)

---

## Can I discard cards voluntarily?
*3 posts · started by luis_camaleon on 2025-06-16* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3528389)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1351710` · 2025-06-16

Can I discard cards voluntarily?
For example, if I have a card I am not interested in, can I discard it before using “preparativos (preparations)” to draw 4 new cards?

Thanks

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-06-16

Yes, you may discard a card without effect at any time. This also applies in the end of turn, when you may draw a card to hand. If you already have 4, you can discard one of them to have space to draw the new card.

---
**#3** · user `1351710` · 2025-06-16

Thank you Jonathan.

## Doubt about ability combination with bjorn
*4 posts · started by Interdaex on 2025-06-08* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3524456)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4208886` · 2025-06-08

When its late Game and i have the bjorns ability to deal X dmg if Monster is in X range, and moreover i have the ability of attack one Monster and the one from behind if the First one is killed and the attack has enough dmg, if i would target a Monster Who is 4 spaces away from me, i throw dices and hit 3, that Monster would be died with 4 impacts and Monster Next to him would receive 3 impacts ?? I mean the dmg is dealed with that ability depends on the distance, when its time to deal remaining dmg with one attack to other Monster Next to him i dont know what dmg should him receive

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-06-09

Attacks are always calculated against a main target. So you target a monster 4 areas away, and therefore deal +4 damage in the attack. Let's say you roll 5 hits in total, and the target only has 2 health. The 3 remaining damage is then dealt to another monster behind it. There are no additional rolls or adjustments of the damage, because that is already determined. This means that this ability (along with similar abilities in Boldur and Embla) are very good at hitting secondary monsters in forests, as you didn't have to take cover into account when rolling.

---
**#3** · user `4208886` · 2025-06-09

Do you mean that ability that deal +4 attack in that case you described, that +4 attack is only for the First Monster, so if u roll 5 hits in total, and the target has 2 health, the First Monster would see +9 dmg, but Monsters behind It just would see 3 dmg ( what remains after the First Monster 5-2). What i mean that this ability that deal as much dmg as areas is the Monster, is just for the First Monster, and for the rest of Monsters that could receive dmg just apply the dmg from the roll

---
**#4** · user `2202341` · 2025-06-13

Hola Jose,
Si estás a rango 4 y sacas 3 impactos en tu ataque, tendrías 7 en total.
Si el primer monstruo tiene 4 de vida, le harías esos 4 de daño y los 3 restantes pasarían directamente al siguiente monstruo (sin preocuparte de cobertura por bosque por ejemplo, es daño directo)

## Doubt about cards in hand
*4 posts · started by Raul_Fernandez_Romo on 2025-06-07* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3523985)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1176743` · 2025-06-07

Hi, I have a doubt about how many cards I can have, since the Spanish manual says that I can only have 4 cards in hand, but I have seen several videos and people have many more cards in their play area.
I don't quite understand this rule of the game.

---
**#2** · user `250362` · 2025-06-07

There are four types of cards:
1) Hero
2) Abilities (Blue) There's no limit of these in your play area. They are not in your hand.
3) Equipment (Green) There's no limit of these in your play area. They are not in your hand.
4) Event (Red) - These are in your hand and your hand limit is four. You can discard an Event card from your hand without using its effect to make room for other event cards.

---
**#3** · user `1176743` · 2025-06-07

Thank you very much, you have solved my doubts.

---
**#4** · user `2756163` · 2025-06-08 *(edited)*

[q="ol_bubba"]There are four types of cards:
1) Hero
2) Abilities (Blue) There's no limit of these in your play area. They are not in your hand.
3) Equipment (Green) There's no limit of these in your play area. They are not in your hand.
4) Event (Red) - These are in your hand and your hand limit is four. You can discard an Event card from your hand without using its effect to make room for other event cards.[/q]
Note than some abilities grant heroes a larger hand size for the Event cards, so it is not uncommon to be able to hold more than 4.
This may also be a source of confusion

---

## Equipment 1 per turn
*2 posts · started by Ralsekx on 2025-05-23* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3516202)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2394389` · 2025-05-23

Hi!
Want to play for the first time today, but reading the rules I didn't understand if you can use each equipment only once for turn... 

Can you use the same weapon more than once? or for additional attacks from event cards there is no limitation about equipment cards?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-05-23

An equipment may both increase your stats and provide an effect. The stats is always active, so if your weapon gives you +2 attack strength, that applies in each attack action. However, some effects are things you *do*, and they may only be used once per turn. If you have - for example - the Quiver in Bjorn's deck. It always gives him +1 attack strength, but he may also use it once per turn to take 1 damage on it to add 1 damage to that attack action.

---

## What exactly comprises a named location 
*2 posts · started by ilpalazo on 2025-05-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3516037)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `414012` · 2025-05-23

Im a bit unclear where places like marsh of sorrow or dead plains begin and end? Is it just where the red outline is? Or is it all areas that have that colour, which goes beyond the red outline?

---
**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-05-23

It is the line that lines the outline of the locations.

It can be a red line (Marsh of Sorrow, Dead Plains etc) or a yellow line (Grimheim, Nailfaire, Troll Caves and Wyrm Lair) 

It is also wise to be clear about terminology of the map in this game. Locations vs areas

The first page of rules in the manual, under Game Board, state:

     All areas with names are called locations. Some locations contain several areas and have a red or yellow border.

---

## Free actions never count as attack actions & Boldur's Rapid strike
*4 posts · started by PeakyBoardgamer on 2025-05-17* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3513201)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2874308` · 2025-05-17

Hello everyone,

I am unsure if this also counts for abilities that grant an attack action like boldur's rapid strike.
am i right?
thanks

---
**#2** · user `2874308` · 2025-05-17

For example if i perform an attack with Rapid strike , would Sweeping strike also apply (it applies to each attack action)? 

Another case is if there is a mission (to gain an equipment) that asks you to spend an attack action. could i gain the equipment by using rapid strike?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-05-17

Rapid Strike tells you to perform an attack action, so that is indeed an actual attack action.
The reason for this rule is to make clear that playing an event card which rolls attack dice, is not an attack action, even if it could be intuitively described as attacking a monster. So we wanted to separate attack actions from other effects that roll dice. In the case of Rapid Strike, however, it specifically tells you to perform an attack action.

Yes, if a quest requires you to spend an attack action, that could be an attack action gained from Rapid Strike.

---
**#4** · user `2874308` · 2025-05-17

Great, I want to stress that in the video! Stay tuned

---

## about using equipment only once
*3 posts · started by ektorakos on 2025-05-17* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3513198)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `191303` · 2025-05-17

Hello everyone,
When saying using equipment only once do we mean only the power or also the dice modifiers?
Lets take bjorns trollbane bow.
It adds +3 dice when attacking and also adds +1 dmg against trollkin.

Lets say i attack a dead enemy. I use the bow and add +3 dice

If by any means i gain a second attack . Am i able to add +3 dice from trollbane? 

Hope it makes sense
Thanks

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-05-17

The stats modifier is permanent, not "activated", so it always applies. If you have several attack actions, you count the strength bonus on all cards each time.

---
**#3** · user `2874308` · 2025-05-17

[q="Lord_Aethan"]The stats modifier is permanent, not "activated", so it always applies. If you have several attack actions, you count the strength bonus on all cards each time.[/q]
Thanks Jonathan.
Amazing game!

## Sweeping strike clarification
*2 posts · started by Biky_One on 2025-05-09* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3509352)

After killing a monster with sweeping strike, if I have enough damages to kill a second monster, can I continue to deal damages to a third monster, or is it just the first target and only one other monster?

---
**#2** · user `154405` · 2025-05-10

From the designer here on bgg :
[i]"It is only 1 additional step: it only chains overkill damage to the next clockwise monster (he could previously cut through several monsters, but it was ultimately deemed too strong. Think of it as him using it in combination with Rapid Strike and it works again)"[/i]
