## Clarification of Bjorn's Trollbane Quest
*3 posts · started by ol_bubba on 2025-05-03* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3506440)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `250362` · 2025-05-03 *(edited)*

Bjorn's Trollbane quest is [u]"Collect 5 gold from killing trollkin [/u]to get a fearsome reputation." We played FATE twice and this came up both times. As Bjorn kills trollkins we have placed the gold on the Trollbane card to keep track of things. Can the Bjorn player use that gold for an upgrade action before completing the quest? We have discussed that we could use red or green gems to keep track of the gold.

---
**#2** · user `36112` · 2025-05-03

You can use the gold whenever you like.  You're just tracking its collection.  Some Quests require you to choose between quest fulfillment and XP gain, but those state so explicitly.

Also, another option --  you could use a damage die to keep track of the quest progress.

---
**#3** · user `250362` · 2025-05-03

Also, another option --  you could use a damage die to keep track of the quest progress.
[/q]

## End of Turn and Event Cards
*3 posts · started by Chr0n0s4 on 2025-05-01* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3505152)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1288909` · 2025-05-01

I assume I cannot play Event cards when I draw them in the „End of Turn Phase“? (E.g cards that deal dmg etc)

---
**#2** · user `1048591` · 2025-05-01

[q="Chr0n0s4"]I assume I cannot play Event cards when I draw them in the „End of Turn Phase“? (E.g cards that deal dmg etc)[/q]
Not in that turn, no, but in next turn (also upcoming monsters turn if they are retaliation)

---
**#3** · user `2756163` · 2025-05-01

[q="Chr0n0s4"]I assume I cannot play Event cards when I draw them in the „End of Turn Phase“? (E.g cards that deal dmg etc)[/q]
Correct, mostly. 

There are a small number of cards that will let the hero avoid damage or resist attacks during the later Monster phase and you can play those cards then.

## Finkel Questions
*3 posts · started by Marco_Armbruster on 2025-04-30* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3504745)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2244733` · 2025-04-30 *(edited)*

Hello,

I really enjoy the Game! Played now almost all Characters in Solo Mode. Yesterday finkel. Two questions Came up:

1. does finkels fireball 2 hurt himself, if he is adjacend to his target? I guess yes.

2. does his healing Horn gear heal 1 dmg each of his turns? I guess yes.

Thanks. :)

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-04-30

If it says "monster" it doesn't damage heroes, but if it says "character" it hurts heroes and monsters alike. 

Yes, his Drink of the Tide heals 1 damage each of his turns.

## Making sure I got enemy movement right
*7 posts · started by Tember on 2025-04-28* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3503701)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1830841` · 2025-04-28 *(edited)*

I’m just double checking that if a monster, say a goblin with charge, does not start adjacent to a hero, then it will use its full movement (3 in the case of goblin with charge) to move towards grimheim (provided it’s not blocked by another figure) even if during the movement it would be adjacent to a hero.  That is to say it would move past a hero and end outside of adjacency even if, during its move, it had been adjacent.  It wouldn’t stop its movement when it became adjacent during the movement right?

Thanks!  Enjoying the game a great deal!

---
**#2** · user `36112` · 2025-04-28

Incorrect - it [u]would[/u] stop if it becomes adjacent to a hero during movement!

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-04-28

No, the Golden rule is that a monster does not move if adjacent to a hero, and that takes effect even in the middle of a movement.

---
**#4** · user `250362` · 2025-04-28

[q="Lord_Aethan"]No, the Golden rule is that a monster does not move if adjacent to a hero, and that takes effect even in the middle of a movement.[/q]
Just to confirm this applies even if the monster is in an adjacent hex "behind" a hero where the monster would have a clear path to move forward otherwise?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#5** · user `430700` · 2025-04-28

Yes, they are locked in melee combat as long as they are adjacent to a hero.

---
**#6** · user `1830841` · 2025-04-28

[q="Lord_Aethan"]No, the Golden rule is that a monster does not move if adjacent to a hero, and that takes effect even in the middle of a movement.[/q]

Thank you!  That helps a lot.  I interpreted the following sentence from the rulebook incorrectly then:

“If a monster is not adjacent to a hero, it will move as normal, even if that means it moves out of attack range.”

I thought this would apply to the middle of the movement, but now I understand this sentence is applying to the case of, say, a fire horde having range 2 attack but not starting adjacent to a hero.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#7** · user `430700` · 2025-04-28

OK, I understand how that might be unclear. Perhaps we need to revise that sentence for a future print, thanks for pointing it out!

---

## Grimheim range
*2 posts · started by Nairibg on 2025-04-27* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3503167)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4225287` · 2025-04-27 *(edited)*

Grimheim is not adjacent to anything, but can it be within range 2?

Finkel has both an ability and a card that lets him move others within range 2.
While standing in Grimheim, can he move anything (himself or another) outside of Grimheim?
While standing in Grimheim can he move another character that stands in Grimheim out of Grimheim?

Are heroes in Grimheim considered adjacent to each other? 
Can you use items/abilities that can be used on adjacent heroes?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-04-27

All heroes in Grimheim are considered adjacent to each other, and cannot interact with characters outside Grimheim. If Finkel is in Grimheim, he may use these effects on himself or another hero inside Grimheim to move them out of there, but he cannot move characters already outside. 

If he is outside Grimheim, her cannot use these effects on heroes inside Grimheim.

---

**#3** · user `1191012` · 2026-04-02

What happens if you draw Legends during game setup? Place them as normal? (I didn't see any rule that says that you set them aside during game setup)

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2026-04-02

That's right, you just place them. Legends are cool, but they are generally not more difficult than other missions. Usually they exchange a LOT of monsters for a cooler one. In most cases, the total headache is the same from a legend and a normal monster card. That can depend greatly on the combinatorics, of course. A legend buffing all of its faction is of course devastating if the board is already full of that faction.

**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-04-27

Neither of your options. 
It will move it’s normal amount of 1 (or 2 if charging due to Monster Die or final game rounds)

If you were behind it and it was 2 spaces away from you, it is now more 3 spaces away so cannot attack you that turn.

So my first guess is right, monster moves forward and doesn't attack me

Yes, the first option is right, the monster will move away from you and can no longer attack you.

## When can you use abilities/items?
*3 posts · started by Nairibg on 2025-04-21* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3500344)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4225287` · 2025-04-22

We had a scenario where Bjorn had 2 things: the skill that lets him heal and item or a hero, and the item that lets him add one damage. The item however was already maxed out on damage tokens (3/3). Bjorn did an attack, is he allowed to throw the dice first and then decide to heal his item to add more damage, or does he have to heal the item before throwing the dice?

---
**#2** · user `36112` · 2025-04-22 *(edited)*

Great question!

I don't have an official answer...however I'll give you my best guess.

I believe the intent is, unless an exception is granted by the rules or by the nature of the effect, that it is not allowed for any Action, be it "Free" or not, to be interrupted by any another action, be that action "Free" or not.

That is to say, I do not believe the Action "Attack" can be interrupted by the Free Action "Use an Ability" (in this example, the one that removes damage).

Note, however, that there are many, many Free Actions that qualify as exceptions -- e.g. the Free Action "Play a Card," to play a card which refers to ”this attack action", or the Free Action "Use an Ability," to use an ability that affects die rolls.

That's my interpretation, but again, it's only a guess.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-04-22

The equipment that lets him add 1 damage to the attack (Quiver) may only be used once per turn, so even if you could repair 1 damage from it, it could still not be used an additional time in the same turn.
Other than that, Anthony is right that actions cannot interrupt each other, with the significant exception of actions which specifically say "this attack action", which may be used within an attack action, or effects which prevent damage, they may be used once per time you receive damage, and effects which otherwise specifically tell you to use them at a specific time.
This means that if you want to keep your options open, you need to repair the equipment before using the attack, if you want to be able to use it for that attack.

---

## Move Towards Grimheim + End movement question
*6 posts · started by ilpalazo on 2025-04-16* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3497389)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `414012` · 2025-04-16

Im like 99% sure the answer to these is yes, but just for sanity check:

1. Seek shelter - if you cannot make into a location, can you still use the card to move two spaces towards it, or is the INTO a requirement?
2. If you roll the monster dice where they push you towards grimheim and you are adjacent to it, do you go INTO Grimheim? This could auto lose you the game towards the end if your heroes are surrounded with their backs to grimheim so to speak. 
3. Boldur has an equipment card whose quest asks him to end their movement next to a level 3 or legend. I assume its not enough for him to simply stay in one place next to a legend without doing a move action or a card that allows him to move?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-04-16

1. Seek Shelter must be into a location. Note that a location is any named area, and some locations are many areas, such as the Marsh of Sorrow. So you may use this card to move 2 steps to any of those areas, perhaps even starting inside that location and moving 2 steps to another area inside the same location. But yes, you must end in the location, otherwise you cannot seek shelter out in the open 🙂
2. Yes, you may be pushed into Grimheim. When you play with the monster dice, you need larger safety margins to play safe.
3. I don't know which equipment this is referring to? If the quest is to "end your movement", it may be any form of movement, either a move action or with an event card that moves, but it is not enough to just stand still.

Cheers!

---
**#3** · user `4225287` · 2025-04-17

1. Is Grimheim considered a location?

3. I believe some cards say "end your movement action", can those be triggered by any movement or does it have to be a movement action? There are cards and a Finkel ability that let you move other characters, if you move other players would that also trigger effects that say "end your movement" or move into or next to type of effects?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-04-18

If it says movement "action" it must be an action, otherwise it could be any movement.

---
**#5** · user `4225287` · 2025-07-15

Would monsters pushing players be considered a movement?  Alva has an upgrade that if she ends any movement in a forest she gained mana or health (I cant remember which), If a monster pushing here into a forest would that be ending any movement?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#6** · user `430700` · 2025-07-16

That's a good question! This question actually never popped up. I would say no, because it is not an active movement, just something that happened to you.

## Sindra upgrades main ability ✅
*3 posts · started by Hetzer6 on 2025-04-16* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3497287)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1394762` · 2025-04-16

I have some trouble understanding the point of her upgraded character card.

The starting ability says that you can spend a movement action to spend 3 mana in order to move anywhere.

The upgraded version says that you can spend [u]any[/u] action to spend 3 mana in order to move anywhere.

What is the benefit? Let's say I spend an attack action. I spend it for the card effect, so the way I understand it I do not make an attack and [u]instead [/u] use 3 mana to move.

German version btw... So maybe it's a translation thing.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430994` · 2025-04-16

> ↳ *Replying to #1 (user `1394762`):* I have some trouble understanding the point of her upgraded character card. The starting ability says that you can spend a movement action to spend 3 mana in order to move anywhere. The upgraded version says that you can…

> You are correct, it is instead. The benefit is mostly the stats, but this also gives you the option to move AND teleport, opening up some interesting options. Especially if you mostly use abilities and cards to take out monsters.
> Cheers!

---
**#3** · user `2044257` · 2026-04-06

It does not happen in every game, but there are situations where Sindra both needs to teleport and move the same round (if for example she wants to both enter a location in order to achieve a quest and stop a group of monsters far away from that location that would otherwise move in Grimheim). In my recent game, I chose the character card upgrade as my first upgrade as I "foresaw" an amazing play the round after the upgrade and it worked out very well.

## Inspire Defense
*4 posts · started by Chris Janiec on 2025-04-11* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3494659)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `29113` · 2025-04-12

Alva's "Inspire Defense" card has you spend 2 mana to add 1 Town piece.  What is the source of this mana?  Focus actions add only to abilities or equipment, and the card does not have its own Mana Generation. [article=45415133][/article]

Cards using mana without an own mana source may use mana from other cards.

you get one mana if your your movement ends in the forest

🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-04-11

The first side says "When you end a move action", the upgraded side says "when you end ANY movement" so on the upgraded side, it doesn't have to be a move action. This is very powerful with her Treetreader ability.

## Card actions  ✅
*2 posts · started by Archstanton1984 on 2025-04-07* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3491995)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2446065` · 2025-04-07

Hello,
I got one more question.
If a card gives you an attack action, are you allowed to use a second attack action in your turn by using one of your two actions or are you them only allowed to take three actions in one turn but they Must be different ones?
Thx

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430994` · 2025-04-07

> ↳ *Replying to #1 (user `2446065`):* Hello, I got one more question. If a card gives you an attack action, are you allowed to use a second attack action in your turn by using one of your two actions or are you them only allowed to take three actions in one…

> If something gives you an attack action, it is a gift so you don't have to 'pay' with your action marker. Also, you can choose the same as one of your action markers, i.e. you can do this extra attack action plus a regular attack action using your marker if you want.
> Other than that, the extra attack action works the same as the regular one and uses your strength value and all other applicable effects.
>
> Cheers!

## Event card limit
*3 posts · started by MatjesHH on 2025-04-03* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3489802)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1282742` · 2025-04-03

If I already have 4 event cards and draw a new event card, do I have to discard one first or can I look at the new card first and then decide which card to discard?

---
**#2** · user `46787` · 2025-04-03

[q="MatjesHH"]If I already have 4 event cards and draw a new event card, do I have to discard one first or can I look at the new card first and then decide which card to discard?[/q]

For the end of turn draw it is specified in the rules:
4. Draw 1 event card to your hand. If you already have 4 cards, you
may not draw this card, unless you discard another card without effect
first

And for the Prepare action it is said, on the same page (6):
Prepare - Draw 1 card from your event deck. You may never
have more than 4 cards in your hand, but you may discard
cards without effect at any time to make room for new cards.


So if there are any more instances of drawing the card I would assume the same applies: discard first if at limit, then draw.

S.

---
**#3** · user `1282742` · 2025-04-03

Thank you, I must have overlooked that.

---

## Ability cards and Mana ✅
*5 posts · started by MatjesHH on 2025-04-03* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3489801)

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430994` · 2025-04-03

> ↳ *Replying to #1 (user `1282742`):* Does an ability card I put into play automatically get mana added to the ability card when that card generates mana? Like with ability cards I upgrade. I saw this in a video.

> At the end of your own turn, all your cards (abilities + equipment) that has a green dot in the bottom corner will gain 1 mana each (or 2 if it says so).
> So yes.

## Red dot on equipment…Precision Axes
*2 posts · started by Rocky123 on 2025-04-01* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3488996)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `194423` · 2025-04-01 *(edited)*

Never mind.. missed it in the rules… 



What does the red dot on Precision Axes mean… there is a red dot followed by : Deal 1 unpreventable.. etc…

Does it mean is can only be used when defending or in the enemy phase?

Thanks

---
**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-04-01

[q="Rocky123"]What does the red dot on Precision Axes mean… there is a red dot followed by : Deal 1 unpreventable.. etc…

Does it mean is can only be used when defending or in the enemy phase?

Thanks [/q]
When you activate the item, the axes lose 1 durability and you place a red crystal in the card to signify that. Their maximum available durability is bottom right which informs you how many times you can use its power. 

Like most items, they can be repaired using event cards that repair items (and remove crystal(s) from the card).

---

## Embla's custom-made armor (Translation from german edition)
*3 posts · started by MatjesHH on 2025-03-30* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3487839)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1282742` · 2025-03-30

How does Embla's custom armor work?
The card says prevent 2 damage, but the card can only absorb 3 damage in total. Does that mean the armor can absorb 2 damage three times? Otherwise, the card makes no sense, since it can only absorb 2 damage once and 1 damage once.

---
**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-03-30

[q="MatjesHH"]How does Embla's custom armor work?
The card says prevent 2 damage, but the card can only absorb 3 damage in total. Does that mean the armor can absorb 2 damage three times? Otherwise, the card makes no sense, since it can only absorb 2 damage once and 1 damage once.[/q]
It works the same as other items that have durability. 
The armour has a durability of 3 (bottom right corner)
It can absorb up to 2 damage per use, but loses durability each use. 
Hence, as per your initial thought,  it can absorb up to 6 damage until it requires repair.

---
**#3** · user `1282742` · 2025-03-30

[q="mark_c"][q="MatjesHH"]How does Embla's custom armor work?
The card says prevent 2 damage, but the card can only absorb 3 damage in total. Does that mean the armor can absorb 2 damage three times? Otherwise, the card makes no sense, since it can only absorb 2 damage once and 1 damage once.[/q]
It works the same as other items that have durability. 
The armour has a durability of 3 (bottom right corner)
It can absorb up to 2 damage per use, but loses durability each use. 
Hence, as per your initial thought,  it can absorb up to 6 damage until it requires repair.[/q]

Tanks a lot.

## Ebla and Firehorde clarification  ✅
*2 posts · started by Rocky123 on 2025-03-29* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3487338)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `194423` · 2025-03-29

Emba used event to kick an enemy one space dealing it damage.. is that space directly away.. specifically if there is an enemy behind it… what happens 

Firehorde can attack 2 spaces away.. does this mean it has like a charge 2 or a ranged attack after it moves if an enemy is 2 away.


Thanks

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430994` · 2025-03-29

> ↳ *Replying to #1 (user `194423`):* Emba used event to kick an enemy one space dealing it damage.. is that space directly away.. specifically if there is an enemy behind it… what happens Firehorde can attack 2 spaces away.. does this mean it has like a cha…

> You can do a sidekick to move it to the side so you can hit it again for example. You can kick it 1 step in any direction that has an available area (no characters).
>
> Firehorde has range 2 so they can shoot over each other. They can still charge, but only if that would put them in range, so only firehorde at 4 steps away will normally charge (putting them 2 steps away and in range). They must still follow their movement path.

---

## Monster attacks 
*3 posts · started by Rocky123 on 2025-03-29* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3487229)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `194423` · 2025-03-29

Might be overthinking this..

Surrounded by 3 monsters.. so the attacks all happen at one.. or do I fight each monster separately…


As some
Masters have different effects 
Thanks..

---
**#2** · user `36112` · 2025-03-29

Each separately.

It also matters because some Heroes can counterattack.  For example, if the middle member of line of 3 Trollkin is eliminated by a counterattack, then the other two Trollkin will no longer receive the extra Trollkin attack buff.

---
**#3** · user `1802828` · 2025-04-04

only when there is NO possible effect at all that would make any difference, then I roll all attack dice at the same time. But this only happens max 10-20%.
else, I roll one attack after another.

e.g. because Boldur does prevent 1 damage of every attack, with that character you can NEVER roll several attacks in one go. otherwise you dont need to roll any attacks that only have one dice.

## Sindra Character Card Ability
*3 posts · started by Lightningbolt1312 on 2025-03-27* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3486293)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1322333` · 2025-03-28 *(edited)*

So far really enjoying this game! Just want to make sure that in order to use Sindra's character starting ability,  she needs to use 3 mana actions to get mana on to the card? All other characters have starting abilities that don't cost mana. 

Just making sure I'm understanding that correctly!

Thanks!

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-03-28

Cards which collect mana must use mana from its own card. However, Sindra doesn't collect mana on her own card, so she can use mana from her other cards. So once you've stored up some mana on your Spark ability, you can use her ability to teleport.

---
**#3** · user `1322333` · 2025-03-28

That is incredibly helpful thank you!!

---

## Rapid Strike - Triggers Attack Action Cards?
*6 posts · started by XeroGaming on 2025-03-26* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3485426)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3985875` · 2025-03-26

I have a question about whether Boldur's Rapid Strike can trigger other cards. The rules say Free Actions never count as an Attack Action. Rapid Strike says perform an Attack Action. So would using Rapid Strike trigger cards like Sweeping Strike and Smiterbiter?

---
**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-03-26

Yes. It specifically allows you to make an attack action, so you get your usual bonuses.

Free actions that let you roll dice to attack an adjacent monster are not attack actions.

---
**#3** · user `3985875` · 2025-03-26

Thanks for clearing that up!

---
**#4** · user `194423` · 2025-04-02

Are we sure this is correct… I like it.. but how else would you use equipment and their abilities (tied to attacking).. the rules say you can only use them once per turn.. If it is an attack that is the once per turn… you never get another attack action uncles it’s by an ability…

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#5** · user `430700` · 2025-04-02

That is correct. Although it is not explicitly stated on the cards, some cards are "activated" to get an effect when you choose so, and they can only be "activated" once per turn. However, some equipment and abilities give you passive buffs or benefits that are always active, such as the attack strength.

---
**#6** · user `3985875` · 2025-04-03

Thank you for confirming!

---

## Question on monster dice (Maneuver)
*2 posts · started by DanielMUC on 2025-03-23* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3483485)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3160074` · 2025-03-23

How does the rotation exactly work (monster dice / Maneuver)?
a) How many steps will the monsters move? Only one hex? 
b) Will they also move if they would leave the path?
c) Will they also move if they would diverge from Grimheim?
Thanks in advance.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-03-23

Hi! The normal movement rules do not apply when rolling the dice, because it is not in the monster movement phase. The rotation explicitly applies to monsters adjacent to heroes, which may not move at all during the movement phase. So when you roll the monster dice, disregard the normal movement rules.

a) Yes, they move 1 area.
b) Yes, they will normally diverge from their path when doing this.
c) Yes, this may cause the monsters to go 1 step further away from Grimheim.

Cheers!

---

## Attacking through/over Grimheim///Seer of Odin attack
*4 posts · started by mrtimppa on 2025-03-23* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3483376)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2698770` · 2025-03-23

Hi, thanks for a wonderful game. after a few games we still have a couple of questions;
1) According to the rulebook Grimheim is considered one big area. Heroes with range 2 attacks could therefore attack a monster standing on the other side of the village? thinking of it like arrows flying over the houses 😊
2) The second level of Seer of Odin deals 1 damage to all heroes everywhere. Is this an attack with infinite range or is it only dealt when she's standing next to a hero?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-03-23

Hi! I am glad you like it! 
There is a passage late in the rules addressing shooting over Grimheim. It cannot be done. If you have - for example - attack range 3, you need to "curve" that shot around Grimheim.
The Seer attacks everyone at the same time and regardless of their distance.

---
**#3** · user `2698770` · 2025-03-23

so to clarify; the seer always attacks?

---

## Blocking Monster Entrance to Grimheim
*3 posts · started by awesomeshotdude on 2025-03-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3482808)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `115818` · 2025-03-22

Considering monsters cannot interact with heroes in Grimheim, and heroes in Grimheim unable to interact with monster outside Grimheim...if I have 2-3 heroes positioned in Grimheim in the hexes where a monsters path would enter Grimheim, essentially blocking any monster's entrance...and there is a monster on that path on the outer edge of Grimheim, what happens. Does the monster just stay there unable to harm the heroes...basically doing nothing until the heroes blocking its access to Grimheim move and thus allow it to enter Grimheim?

---
**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-03-22

As you stated, there is no interaction, so a character does not block the monsters incursion and you lose a town piece.

(Also, the "hexes" in the town are not individual areas but all together count as one area)

---
**#3** · user `115818` · 2025-03-23

[q="mark_c"]As you stated, there is no interaction, so a character does not block the monsters incursion and you lose a town piece.

(Also, the "hexes" in the town are not individual areas but all together count as one area)[/q]

Thanks for the reply, much appreciated :)

## Equipment cards with damage
*4 posts · started by MatjesHH on 2025-03-22* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3482722)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1282742` · 2025-03-22 *(edited)*

I have a few questions about Equipment cards.

If I have a card that prevents damage, I can only use that card when I'm attacked. That's clear to me.

But how can I use, for example, Embla's Equipment card "Lightfooted - Move 1 Space" (I have the German version and hope the card title is correct)?

If I understand correctly, I can take a damage crystal on my turn and place it on the card to move one space. Can I also use the card when I'm attacked?

For example, if three monsters are adjacent to me and the first attack causes damage to me, can I then place the damage on that card and move one space to prevent the other two monsters from attacking me?

Could I then use Embla's "Throwing Knife" in response to an attack in the same way or take a damge crystal in my turn and use the card?

Brilliant game, by the way. Thanks Jonathan.

---
**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-03-22

[q="MatjesHH"]I have a few questions about Equipment cards.

If I have a card that prevents damage, I can only use that card when I'm attacked. That's clear to me.

But how can I use, for example, Embla's Equipment card "Lightfooted - Move 1 Space" (I have the German version and hope the card title is correct)?

If I understand correctly, I can take a damage crystal on my turn and place it on the card to move one space. Can I also use the card when I'm attacked?

For example, if three monsters are adjacent to me and the first attack causes damage to me, can I then place the damage on that card and move one space to prevent the other two monsters from attacking me?

Could I then use Embla's "Throwing Knife" in response to an attack in the same way or take a damge crystal in my turn and use the card?

Brilliant game, by the way. Thanks Jonathan.

[/q]
The situation you described is not possible (Using the effect of the equipment card during the monster's phase of the game)

There are a limited number of Event cards that can be played to avoid damage during the monster phase, and the ability to do so is printed upon the card itself.

---
**#3** · user `1282742` · 2025-03-22

[q="mark_c"][q="MatjesHH"]I have a few questions about Equipment cards.

If I have a card that prevents damage, I can only use that card when I'm attacked. That's clear to me.

But how can I use, for example, Embla's Equipment card "Lightfooted - Move 1 Space" (I have the German version and hope the card title is correct)?

If I understand correctly, I can take a damage crystal on my turn and place it on the card to move one space. Can I also use the card when I'm attacked?

For example, if three monsters are adjacent to me and the first attack causes damage to me, can I then place the damage on that card and move one space to prevent the other two monsters from attacking me?

Could I then use Embla's "Throwing Knife" in response to an attack in the same way or take a damge crystal in my turn and use the card?

Brilliant game, by the way. Thanks Jonathan.

[/q]
The situation you described is not possible (Using the effect of the equipment card during the monster's phase of the game)

There are a limited number of Event cards that can be played to avoid damage during the monster phase, and the ability to do so is printed upon the card itself.[/q]
Thank you, That means i can use these cards only in my turn and i have to take a damage crystal from the Stock to use the ability, right?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-03-22

The ability card doesn't use markera at all, but each ability may only be used once per turn. So with Fleetfoot, Embla may move 1 area each turn, and that movement is not part of a move action. Using abilities and equipment and playing events are all free actions, and actions may only be used on your turn, except if they specify otherwise. Cheers!

---

## Can I use Event Cards multiple times on my turn, or only once like Abilities and Equipment Cards?
*2 posts · started by Marder12 on 2025-03-21* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3482168)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4205627` · 2025-03-21

Can I use Eventcards multiple times on my turn, or only once like Abilities and Equipment Cards?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-03-21

When you play an event card, it is discarded, so they are one-time use, but if you have more cards, you may play more cards. In the same way, you may only use each equipment once per turn, but if you have several equipment, each one may be used.

---

## Firehorde, focus on attack or Grimheim ✅
*4 posts · started by Nytramist on 2025-03-16* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3479131)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4200980` · 2025-03-16

Normally the movement stops adjacent to a hero and the attack of the monster follows. But how about the firehorde with range 2: if an hero stands not between the monster and Grimheim, but lets say on the right or left side of the firehorde, will the firehorde charge to get the attack or is the focus still on Grimheim? Will the movement of the firehorde to Grimheim stops, if an attack to the right/left side with range 2 is possible - the hero is not adjacent and stands not in the way.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-03-16

No, the movement only stops if a hero is adjacent, or if the movement path is blocked. If none of those apply, the monster moves, even if that means it can no longer attack.

---
**#3** · user `4200980` · 2025-03-16

Thank you for the reply. That also means that a firehorde will not charge to get the attack to the right/left side, if the hero not stands in the way to Grimheim?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430994` · 2025-03-16

> ↳ *Replying to #3 (user `4200980`):* Thank you for the reply. That also means that a firehorde will not charge to get the attack to the right/left side, if the hero not stands in the way to Grimheim?

> [q="Nytramist"]Thank you for the reply. That also means that a firehorde will not charge to get the attack to the right/left side, if the hero not stands in the way to Grimheim?[/q]
> The fire horde will only charge if that puts them in range to attack a player. With their range of 2, it can result in a charge if they are 4 steps away (2steps + 2 range). It also depends on if their movement path takes them closer to a player.
>
> Cheers!

---

## Event Cards : Sneakers (french version unclear)
*4 posts · started by King Bing on 2025-03-13* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3477418)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `154405` · 2025-03-13 *(edited)*

The french version of the card says :
[i]" If a Trollkin monster is on the board, place a brute next to it "[/i]
So it looks like you must place a brute next to each Trollkin monster. It can be very painful. But it is a red card, so why not. 

But the english version of the card says :
[i]" If there is any Trollkin monster on the board, place a brute next to one "[/i]
It looks like you place only one brute next to one Trollkin monster of your choice. It seems more reasonable, but maybe too light for a red card.

So, what is the good way to apply the effect of that event card ?
Thanks ! (great game !)

ps: same thing for the two other cards with same effect for the other two monster types, Fire Horde and Dead (I don't know their names in english)

---
**#2** · user `2756163` · 2025-03-13

The English version of the game is the developed functional version so iIm pretty sure it is the reference version. 

Errant or arbitrary translations like this one where there is a difference in implementation should be adapted back to the English version.

Therefore one brute should be placed and it is your choice which Trillin gets it and which square.

---
**#3** · user `154405` · 2025-03-13

OK, thanks.
And yes, I was sure the English version is correct, but since my English isn't very good, I was afraid I might miss an important nuance.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-03-13

It is only 1 brute, but all event cards also draw another monster card, so it doesn't matter much that it is a red card because another one will be drawn in addition to it.

## Sweeping Strike for multiple attack actions clarification 
*3 posts · started by GameNashon on 2025-03-12* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3477235)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2385352` · 2025-03-12

Hello,

Just wanted to confirm that I understood the card correctly. Sweeping strike lets me add 1 damage to each attack and deal remaining damage to a second monster.

Am I correct in understanding that the second monster has to be adjacent to me and if I have 2 attacks, the effect is active for both attacks (+1 damage and dealing damage to second monster) and this doesn’t mean that I’ve used the card twice. It’s just an ongoing effect?

Thank you for your time

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-03-13

That's right! The card applies in each attack action. Cheers!

---
**#3** · user `2756163` · 2025-03-13

... although note that it has to specifically be the Attack action itself (plus any bonus Attack action Boldur may have) that gains the bonus.

It can't be applied to another effect or ability that allows the character to "attack" a monster by rolling dice against it

---

## Legend movement ✅
*4 posts · started by scotlandbc on 2025-03-11* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3476529)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `52433` · 2025-03-11

This is my final rules question clarification request.  The rules state, "Legends don't like to stand in line behind other monsters. If other monsters stand in their way, they simply switch places with them in order to move..."  If the Legend is at the back of the line behind three monsters, following movement rules the three monsters ahead of the Legend will each move first and the Legend last. No one is technically blocked as the ones in the front move first and clear room for the following ones including the Legend. So they can all move without being blocked. Please explain at what point does the Legend move ahead of the other monsters? Is it anytime a Legend is placed in a column, it automatically exchanges place with the one in the front of the column?  It is a bit unclear to me. Thanks. Bruce

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430994` · 2025-03-11

> ↳ *Replying to #1 (user `52433`):* This is my final rules question clarification request. The rules state, "Legends don't like to stand in line behind other monsters. If other monsters stand in their way, they simply switch places with them in order to mo…

> [q="scotlandbc"]This is my final rules question clarification request.  The rules state, "Legends don't like to stand in line behind other monsters. If other monsters stand in their way, they simply switch places with them in order to move..."  If the Legend is at the back of the line behind three monsters, following movement rules the three monsters ahead of the Legend will each move first and the Legend last. No one is technically blocked as the ones in the front move first and clear room for the following ones including the Legend. So they can all move without being blocked. Please explain at what point does the Legend move ahead of the other monsters? Is it anytime a Legend is placed in a column, it automatically exchanges place with the one in the front of the column?  It is a bit unclear to me. Thanks. Bruce[/q]
> It is correct that in most circumstances this ability does not apply, since the potentially blocking monsters move first.
> However, Heroes can block their path and then the legend will not be stuck behind other monsters. Same on the roads when monster paths converge: this can cause 'traffic jams' but the legends will still make their way forward, right through the traffic jam.
>
> Cheers!

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-03-11

And don't forget the charge. Let's say there is a monster standing in front of a legend. That monster moves first 1 area, and it is now adjacent to a hero. The legend then moves with charge, swapping places with the monster in his way.

---
**#4** · user `177170` · 2025-03-23

Does the legend also swap position with the monster in front of it, if the movement of that monster is blocked for example by an hero ability (German card name: Sperrfeuer )?

## Clarification of when you can play cards outside of your turn.
*5 posts · started by scotlandbc on 2025-03-10* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3475928)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `52433` · 2025-03-10

Played a few times now and am really enjoying the game. Always ends in a close finish. I am not sure I understand when I can play cards outside of my turn. The rules state, “ You may not play cards outside of your turn unless the card specifically tells you to do so or prevents damage.”  Please clarify rule and provide examples of cards that can be played outside of your turn. Thanks. Bruce

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-03-10

The card Retaliation (Embla) for example, says that after a monster attacked you, you deal 2 damage to it. Since monsters only attack on their turn, you will have to play this card outside your turn. She also has the card Vigilance which states that it should be played after the monster movement. So those are examples of cards that can be played outside your turn.

---
**#3** · user `52433` · 2025-03-10

Thanks Jonathan. And in the same fashion, a card that specifically "prevents damage" would naturally occur during the monster attack phase and would state such on the card.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-03-10

The case of preventing damage is implicitly saying it can be played when damage is dealt to you, whenever that might be. For brevity, we only say "Prevent 2 damage."

---
**#5** · user `52433` · 2025-03-11

Got it.  The examples help a lot. Thanks for your quick responses to my questions.

---

## Boldur Eitri Axe and Alva multishot
*4 posts · started by Quriel on 2025-03-03* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3471707)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2888880` · 2025-03-03

Hi, I have the game in French and I think there is a translation issue. If someone could confirm my understanding, that would be great.

I don't know the original name of the card but I have a weapon call "pioche d'Eitri" (I guess in English it should be: "Eitri's Axe") this card says that when you use a quick strike (Frappe rapide) add 2 axe (I guess dice) to the attack action.
Problem: in the french version, there are no card mentionned quick strike (Frappe rapide) I guess it is refering to the basic capacity named "coup rapide". Is that correct?

Another question is regarding Alva card probably named multishot in English. We can choose 2 monster within range and lanuch 2 (attack symbol) on each of them.
Does that mean we can do two full attack? or we launch 2 dice on each of them?

Thanks
So far, love the game.
Quentin

---
**#2** · user `4011800` · 2025-03-03

First question: that is correct, the axe says whenever you use the base ability (another attack action) you are granted an additional 2 dice (the axe itself grants 2 dice on all attack actions as well). 

Second question: you get to roll 2 dice against 2 separate monsters within range.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-03-04

That's right, thanks @DeliriumtheEndless!
Note that only attack actions count as "attacks". Equipment and event cards that deal standalone damage or roll dice are not considered attacks.

---
**#4** · user `2888880` · 2025-03-04

Great! Thanks for the answers!

## Windbite Quest: Attack Range 4
*3 posts · started by rswoboda on 2025-03-01* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3470471)

**#2** · user `4011800` · 2025-03-01

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-03-01

The game is made in English, so the English version is correct. You need to kill 4 monsters at range 2 or more.

## Seek Shelter
*4 posts · started by DeliriumtheEndless on 2025-02-25* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3467752)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4011800` · 2025-02-25

After playing several times and reading through the rules questions here it appears that the cards generally behave the way they're written. 

So I just wanted to make sure Seek Shelter is the same. The card says "You may not move more this turn". We took it to mean you may not move more after playing the card, neither using a move action or playing other cards that allow you to move (such as Maneuver). Is this correct? 

There is a possible way to read the card that if you intend to play it you are not allowed to move in any other way that turn (thus removing the possibility of using a move action or playing Maneuver BEFORE using Seek Shelter). But with the way other cards and rules behave, the game and cards are usually more straightforward and "simple" than that.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-02-25

That is correct, the restriction applies after using the card :)

---
**#3** · user `1511148` · 2025-02-25

I have a more basic, and likely somewhat ignorant question. I don't understand "Move up to 2 areas into a location." Does the character need to be next to the location, or is this more like a teleport of sorts? I thought at first that the best use was: take movement action first for three spaces, then this card for two more. But I remain confused!

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-02-25

It is basically 2 additional areas, with the requirement that they end in a location. If you stand next to a location, such as the Highlands, then you may move 2 areas into it, you don't have to stop as soon as you enter. In fact, if you already stand in the Highlands, you may use this to move 2 areas to another area inside the Highlands location.

---

## Draugr armor vs multiple damage dealing cards and abilities
*3 posts · started by Sethlawl on 2025-02-24* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3467335)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3976723` · 2025-02-24

Heya, we find those armored Draugr beasts hardest to handle so we have a question about how exactly the armor works in a specific situations:

I'll give an example with Finkel - let's say I have the Fireball II ability that also deals 1 damage to adjacent monsters, the Deja Vu ability that performs the effect of a card twice, I have the Lightning rod that allows me to spend one mana to deal one additional damage to whatever target I deal damage to and I have the Rain of fire card that allows me to deal 1 damage to each adjacent monster. 

I am standing next to 2 Draugr and I use Fireball on one of them, followed with double Rain of fire and I have mana to spare for the Lightning rod effect. 
If I roll 5 hits Is it correct to assume the Draugr that is the main target of the fireball is dealt 4 damage and prevents all the other +1 damage effects, i.e. double rain of fire plus the Lightning rod damage, while the other Draugr is completely unaffected by all the hassle happening right next to him? It would seem a bit more useful if we can add the Lightning rod effect to the current damage dealt, but the way I understand the wording the case is not so and I have to feel useless against those 2 armored giants?

Also out of curiosity - what led to the decision to name those monsters dead instead of undead, I would imagine both were an option at some point? :)

---
**#2** · user `4011800` · 2025-02-26

I am not 100% certain, but given how the rules are written, how timings work, and how cards work, I would say the following:

Fireball is a free action. Rain of Fire is a free action. But they're separate free actions and therefore deal damage separately from one another. 

Lightning Rod can add 1 damage each time you deal damage (given mana reserves of course), but this does not appear to be a separate event. It is simply added to the same event already dealing damage. Likewise Armor removes 1 damage each time damage is dealt. 

In your case, I would say: 
Fireball would damage monster 1 with 5 damage. Armor would remove 1 damage. Lightning Rod can add 1 damage. 
Fireball splash would damage monster 2 with 1 damage. Armor would remove 1 damage. Lightning Rod can add 1 damage. 
It seems Armor and Lightning Rod would cancel each other out (if you have the mana to spend). Monter 1 would in that case be dealt 5 damage (and die) and monster 2 would be dealt 1 damage from the splash.

Based on the following thread ( [article=45679528][/article] ) and answer by Jacob I would argue:
Rain of Fire would do 1 damage to monster 1. Armor would remove 1 damage. Lightning Rod can add 1 damage.
Rain of Fire would do 1 damage to monster 2. Armor would remove 1 damage. Lightning Rod can add 1 damage.
It seems that again Armor and Lightning Rod would cancel each other out (if you have the mana to spend). Both monsters would be dealt 1 damage if you spend the mana.

Déja Vu would then trigger Rain of Fire again.
Rain of Fire (Déja Vu) would damage monster 1. Armor would remove 1 damage. Lightning Rod can add 1 damage.
Rain of Fire (Déja Vu) would damage monster 2. Armor would remove 1 damage. Lightning Rod can add 1 damage.
It seems that again Armor and Lightning Rod would cancel each other out (if you have the mana to spend). Both monsters would again be dealt 1 damage if you spend the mana.

In total, with 3 of mana spent, you could technically deal 1 (Fireball splash: 1+1-1) + 1 (Rain of Fire: 1+1-1) + 1 (Déja Vu: 1+1-1) damage to monster 2. Without mana then yes Armor would remove the splash, and both Rain of Fire damage events. With 4 mana spent in total, monster 1 would also die from the original Fireball damage (5+1-1) while monster 2 would take 3 damage.

---
**#3** · user `3976723` · 2025-02-27

Thank you for the thorough reply, I imagined it should work exactly the way you describe it, however while most cards say "add this much damage to your attack" the Lightning rod card says "deal one additional damage", and that should lead to armor always mitigating the effect, so I'm hoping for an official confirmation how the card is supposed to work. 

Because like some other people I also assumed that Boldur's Dwarf mail prevents a whole attack action until it turned out it only prevents one damage. I blame the mithril chain mail from a certain movie for that misunderstanding though :D

---

## What is the difference between the red and yellow borders on locations on the map?
*8 posts · started by scotlandbc on 2025-02-21* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3465565)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `52433` · 2025-02-21

Just played for the first time last night. Had a great time. Came back from what appeared to be sure defeat to win! I noticed that some locations on the map are bordered by a red line. Others are bordered by yellow lines. I understand that the yellow ones define locations where the warriors can go. Other than that, are there any other differences between the red and yellowed bordered locations? Why use two colors?  Thanks.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-02-21

The main reason is actually for visual clarity. Some locations are adjacent to eachother, and having red frames for both would not be clear when they share some edges. So there is no actual game-play difference. We use the yellow for the smaller locations which might otherwise be hard to find, while the red borders are for the along-the-edge spawn zones. The smallest locations, the Witch Cabin, the Robber Camp, and the Temple Ruins, have no border at all, because they are a single area.

---
**#3** · user `52433` · 2025-02-22

Thanks Jonathan for the quick response and explanation. Makes sense. Looking forward to my next play.

---
**#4** · user `250362` · 2025-06-10 *(edited)*

I would like confirmation that heroes can cross red lines and go into spawn areas. I have been playing that they can cross red lines.

---
**#5** · user `2756163` · 2025-06-10

[q="ol_bubba"]I would like confirmation that heroes can cross red lines and go into spawn areas. [/q]
Yes they can. 
Just not into Mountain areas

Many of the Quests require a hero to be in a specific place eg Marsh Of Sorrow, to gain an item.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#6** · user `430700` · 2025-06-10

Indeed, the only special thing about locations is that they have names, they are ordinary areas in every other respect. The lines just delineate where those locations are. There is also no difference between yellow lines and red lines, other than to separate them from each other when they share one or more borders.

---
**#7** · user `1881095` · 2025-08-14

It's just mountains we can't enter?..   saw another thread claiming that we also can't enter water...

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#8** · user `430700` · 2025-08-15

Heroes cannot enter mountains. No character may enter water.

## Finkel - Fire Spark ability: damage only on rolled ‘Runes’ or also on rolled ‘hit’
*2 posts · started by mark_c on 2025-02-18* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3463580)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2756163` · 2025-02-18 *(edited)*

Finkel’s Fire Spark ability card invoked a discussion last night.

Card text level 1 (level 2 similar but more powerful): "Cost 2 Mana: roll 3 attack dice against an adjacent monster where Runes count as hits" 

Does he cause damage only by the number of Runes rolled on the attack dice, or is it the number of Hit icons (dependant on cover) plus Rune icons?

Based on the text, we ruled it was only damage due to the number of Runes rolled as it is a spell effect, but this leaves the ability quite underpowered. 
With only one face of each attack die having a Rune, there is a 58% chance of nil damage with three dice being rolled. (And, of course only a 1 in 216 chance of 3 damage)
Even with the upgraded 2nd level Ability and four dice rolled, 48% of uses would statistically cause zero damage, and only 1 in 1296 chance of 4 damage so it is still a weak ability.

If we include Hit and Rune icons, then the ability is perhaps overpowered, especially when combined with a Wizard’s Hat (which lets one roll an extra die each time.)
With 3 dice and including both Hit and Rune icons: 12.5% of rolls do 3 damage, 37.5% 2 damage, 37.5% 1 damage, 12.5% zero damage.

I suspect we played it correctly and the card should read:
‘Cost 2 Mana: roll 3 attack dice against an adjacent monster where [i]only [/i]Runes count as hits"

ps Still enjoying this game with it’s plentiful variety.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-02-18

Runes _also_ count as hits. Thanks for the feedback!

---

## A Dice Roll
*6 posts · started by LemonyFresh on 2025-02-16* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3462619)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `36112` · 2025-02-17 *(edited)*

Declare Attack Action
Attack with 3 dice, 2 Runes appear
Play Mastery (Add 4 dice to this attack action)
Roll 4 dice, 1 Rune appears
Play Piercing Arrows (Play after one of your dice rolls, add 1 damage for each Rune)

Question: How much damage does Piercing Arrows add?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-02-17

3. For the sake of simplicity, the dice roll consists of all dice currently visible from your roll. So Mastery adds 4 dice to the attack roll. However, if you play Perfect Aim to re-roll all misses, that includes runes, they would no longer count of you play Piercing Arrows afterwards.

---
**#3** · user `36112` · 2025-02-17

Ok - so, how does that definition work with Alva's main Weapon, e.g., which rolls a die for each Rune showing, when a Rune is rolled?  That seems like a passive ability which triggers as often as relevant during a turn.

So:

- Roll the Main attack
- 2 Runes are rolled
--- roll 2 more dice immediately
- Play Mastery, adding 4 dice, 1 Rune is rolled
- Do you now roll _3_ more extra dice, because a Rune is rolled, and you assess the whole "die roll", which now contains 3 Runes?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#4** · user `430700` · 2025-02-17

Alva's main weapon triggers off of rolling the runes, and you still only roll the runes once, even if they count to the same dice roll in total. So if you attack and roll 2 runes, you immediately roll 2 more dice. If one of them shows a rune, you roll another die. If you then play Mastery and roll 3 runes, you roll an additional 3 dice. Then you would be glad to have Piercing arrows, which would add 6 damage more to the attack.

---
**#5** · user `36112` · 2025-02-17

...but if instead you did do Perfect Aim, you would then roll that entire collection of Rune + Blank dice, correct?  And potentially then roll more and more if Runes are rolled?

(and THEN play Piercing Arrows, on whatever Runes display at the end of all the rolling?)

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#6** · user `430700` · 2025-02-17

Yes, so in this scenario it definitely matters in which order you play the cards.

---

## Can the Fire Horde attack over other enemies?
*2 posts · started by Doujou on 2025-02-15* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3461953)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3067184` · 2025-02-16 *(edited)*

How do the rules work for attacking through enemies / heroes with range?

---
**#2** · user `36112` · 2025-02-16 *(edited)*

No heroes / enemies block ranged attacks for either side in any way.  If you're surrounded by two concentric circles of Fire Horde, you're getting attacked by all of them.  I suggest sending in the Dwarf.

Note, however, that ranged attacks cannot be traced through any part of Grimheim (i.e. the town in the center of the Map).  One could shoot a long-range bendy arrow [i]around[/i] it, though.

---

## Grimheim: Adjecent areas and moving
*3 posts · started by SvenTheMan on 2025-02-14* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3460899)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2907264` · 2025-02-14

Hi, 
If I am standing in Grimheim, are all adjacent fields considered adjacent? If not, how do I move in Grimheim (to prevent enemys from enterkng) and what do I need to bear in mind if there are several players in Grimheim?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-02-14

If you are in Grimheim, you are not able to interact in any way with characters outside of it. So you do not prevent them from moving, you cannot attack them, and they cannot attack you. To prevent them from moving in, you need to go out of Grimheim and stand in their way (perhaps behind them).

---
**#3** · user `250362` · 2025-02-14

[q="Lord_Aethan"]If you are in Grimheim, you are not able to interact in any way with characters outside of it. So you do not prevent them from moving, you cannot attack them, and they cannot attack you. To prevent them from moving in, you need to go out of Grimheim and stand in their way (perhaps behind them).[/q]
😲😱

---

## Boldur: Focus
*2 posts · started by SvenTheMan on 2025-02-14* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3460895)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2907264` · 2025-02-14

HI, Can I use the Focus card (event deck) and get the Battle Boots at the same time with spending ohne Focus action?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-02-14

Hi Sven,

no, when you spend an action for a quest, you always forfeit that action to get the equipment instead. If you use your focus action for the quest, it gives only that. If you use it for the Focus event card, it gives you only that.

There is one caveat though. Some cards trigger when you perform an action, and those will trigger even if that action is used to complete a quest. For example, if you have an equipment which says "After each attack action....", and then use an attack action to complete a quest, that is still an attack action and still triggers that effect.

Cheers!

---

## What exactly does "spending" an action mean?
*2 posts · started by gubel on 2025-01-28* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3449923)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3654086` · 2025-01-28

I am not a native english speaker and I couldn't finde the question anywhere else here, so what exactly does "spending" an action mean?

For example:
The card DUALIN'S PICK reads "Spend an attack action to gain 1 gold, 1 mana and draw a card."

Does ist mean:
a) You get 1 gold, 1 mana and a card, everytime you use your attack action for an attack?
or
b) You get 1 gold, 1 mana and a card, when you use your attack action, but you may not attack with it in this case?


Thanks! ☺️✌️

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-28

In this game, "spending" an action means performing the action without its normal effect. You basically forfeit the action. However, it still counts as performing that action.
So in the case of Dvalin's Pick:
Boldur may choose to spend an attack action for this effect. He moves an action marker to the attack action space, but does not attack any monster. Instead, he gains 1 gold, 1 mana, and draws 1 card. If Boldur had any effect saying "After each attack action, deal 1 damage", that would still trigger, because this is still an attack action, even though it is not the normal effect.

This is why I use different actions for different quests, because most of the quests correspond to doing something similar to the action, thematically.

---

## Equipment durability
*2 posts · started by Heive1 on 2025-01-28* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3449911)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4046416` · 2025-01-28

Hi!

I was wondering if u can use the +1 roll of an broken equipment. For example the wand which has the effect and +1 roll and the effect costs 1 dmg per use. Can I use the wand's attack roll even if it already has 2 damages and its durability limit is 2?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-28

Hi! The equipment is not "broken" by having damage on it. The only thing that happens due to damage is that you cannot use effects that require you to damage it further. So yes, the attack strength modifier on equipment always applies.

---

## Finkel’s Fireball 2 and Element Ring 
*3 posts · started by AndrejMk1 on 2025-01-27* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3449387)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `4145181` · 2025-01-27 *(edited)*

If a person is playing as Finkel, and they’ve upgraded to Fireball 2 and earned the Element Ring, when they attack an enemy with Fireball 2, do the main target and the adjacent enemies all take an extra damage as part of the ‘attack action’, because of the Element Ring effect, so that, excluding other equipment which can increase damage and the Draugrs’ armor, the adjacent enemies receive 2 damage?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-27

The attack action is always directed at a single target. The element ring adds 1 damage to the attack action against that target. The Fireball II modifier is unaffected.

---
**#3** · user `4145181` · 2025-01-27

Darn! 
Thanks for the quick reply sir!

---

## Stonesoul II and Sindra's character card ✅
*8 posts · started by NateTGreat on 2025-01-26* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3448775)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1694971` · 2025-01-26

For Sindra's Stonesoul II ability, can it be used multiple times in a turn? It says once per monster. Does that mean ever? Or on that turn? Also where does the mana come from to use Sindra's ability from her character card?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-26

An ability card may be used once per turn. This card modified this to say once per monster, but the "per turn" is still valid. So it is once per monster per turn.

As for using mana: mana on the own card must be used, but if the card cannot have mana, but still has an effect that uses mana, it can be paid with mana from anywhere.

---
**#3** · user `39503` · 2025-02-22

[q="Lord_Aethan"]An ability card may be used once per turn. This card modified this to say once per monster, but the "per turn" is still valid. So it is once per monster per turn.

As for using mana: mana on the own card must be used, but if the card cannot have mana, but still has an effect that uses mana, it can be paid with mana from anywhere.[/q]
ah!
this changes a lot as we have been playing to fill her from the event cards and meditation becomes very important.
in this way it is easier but you need to be careful on overuse

---
**#4** · user `36112` · 2025-02-23

A reminder of something somewhat similar that may be easy to forget:

[b]Cards which prevent damage can be used multiple times each turn,[/b] however, [b]only ONCE per instance of damage.[/b]

So, shield up against multiple hits per turn...but be careful to not fill up a piece of equipment with damage after a single smash happens against you.

---
**#5** · user `4225287` · 2025-04-17

To clarify, abilities that says once per monster per turn, can be used multiple times, just not on the same monster?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#6** · user `430700` · 2025-04-18

Yes

> It's once per turn on level 1. The 'once per monster' means you can use it multiple times on your turn, but only once per monster. Next turn you can hit them again if you have the mana to do it.

## Smiterbiter + Sweeping Strike, what to do exactly with excess/remaining damage
*7 posts · started by Felizwerg on 2025-01-26* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3448449)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `2069436` · 2025-01-26 *(edited)*

I just played Boldur for the first time, and I had both the Smiterbiter weapon and the Sweeping Strike ability. Sweeping Strike says "If an adjacent monster is killed in your attack action, any remaining damage may be dealt to a second monster in clockwise order."
Smiterbiter says "If you kill a monster in an attack action, any excess damage may be stored here (max 3 stored). Damage stored here may be added to your attack action."
So, if I kill a monster and deal more damage than needed, do I trigger both cards, so that I deal the remaining damage to a monster in clockwise order AND store the same amount of excess damage (whatever the difference between remaining and excess may be, to me these words mean the same in this context) on the Smiterbiter? I didn't play it that way, since I thought it was really strong and I instead kept using Sweeping Strike to immediately deal the remaining damage to the next monster in clockwise order, so that there was no "excess damage" left. If there hadn't been another monster adjacent to me, or if I just wanted to store the excess damage on Smiterbiter, I could have done that instead of using Sweeping Strike, I think, but probably not both?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-26

You played correctly. "Excess damage" is basically damage beyond what could be dealt, but if your sweeping strike goes against a second monster, the damage is dealt to that monster, so it isn't "excess damage". If you deal 5 damage and cut through 2 monsters with 2 health each, you would have 1 "excess damage".

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-01-26

Also, thank you for your unboxing video, I liked it!

---
**#4** · user `2069436` · 2025-01-26

[q="Lord_Aethan"]You played correctly. "Excess damage" is basically damage beyond what could be dealt, but if your sweeping strike goes against a second monster, the damage is dealt to that monster, so it isn't "excess damage". If you deal 5 damage and cut through 2 monsters with 2 health each, you would have 1 "excess damage".[/q]
Thanks for the quick reply, happy I played it correctly 🙂

---
**#5** · user `2069436` · 2025-01-26

[q="Lord_Aethan"]Also, thank you for your unboxing video, I liked it![/q]

I've only played the game solo so far (once with Embla, once with Boldur), and it flows super smoothly, turns are quick and I love having a cool one-shot co-op game now (most of my co-op games are big campaign ones, so definitely harder to get to the table often)😄

---
**#6** · user `2756163` · 2025-02-17

[q="Felizwerg"][q="Lord_Aethan"]Also, thank you for your unboxing video, I liked it![/q]
Thanks, happy to hear that😊
I've only played the game solo so far (once with Embla, once with Boldur), and it flows super smoothly, turns are quick and I love having a cool one-shot co-op game now (most of my co-op games are big campaign ones, so definitely harder to get to the table often)😄[/q]
Playing "Solo" one can still have 1-4 characters.....
Having one character would be the most difficult I think, despite the built-in scaleability of the game: Less reactivity to subsequent spawnings happening in multiple places across the map.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#7** · user `430700` · 2025-02-17

Playing 1 vs 4 heroes is difficult in different ways:
1) With 1 hero, you must face whatever the game throws at you, while with 4 heroes, each hero can face the kind of monsters he/she is best suited to face.
2) With 1 hero, you must spend considerable time moving to protect Grimheim, while 4 heroes generally have an easier time maneuvering the map.
3) With 1 hero, you only draw 1 monster card per reinforcement turn, and you still have 4 houses to play with, meaning you can easily let 1-3 large monsters enter Grimheim without losing the game, which is a much higher percentage than with 4 players.
4) With 4 heroes, the map is considerably more filled with monsters, such that it will eventually be hard to even find an area to stand which is not a dangerous spot. In solo play, your foes are usually pretty lined up, and you can flank them without worrying too much about other monsters attacking you from the side.

Solo is more prone to luck, and it is more important which character you are playing. The wizards are quite difficult to play in solo due to their fragility. They work best when they have a sturdy defender to hold the grounds while they develop their potential. With 3-4 players, almost any configuration of heroes is equal in difficulty.

---

## Which terrain type is Grimheim ? -> Update  : Question extended

Treetreader can move into - or out of - a forest area. So if you are standing in a forest next to Grimheim, you can move out of that forest into Grimheim.

## Burning Aura, Event card - Finkel
*3 posts · started by ThomasWillinger on 2025-01-21* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3445167)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1281886` · 2025-01-21

The card text is:
"After each step you take this turn, you and every adjacent character take 1 unpreventable damage."

What is a step in this game? I didnt find it mentioned in the rules. 
Is it each action? Is using an ability also an extra step? Is using another event card also another step?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-21

A step is a movement from one area to another. So in a move action, you may move up to 3 areas, each such movement is one step.

---
**#3** · user `1281886` · 2025-01-21

Ah, got it, thanks

## Monster Die - Push
*6 posts · started by Zottelbart on 2025-01-20* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3444693)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1837075` · 2025-01-20

Can the monsters push you into Grimheim?
Lost in the last round just because of this die result :(

---
**#2** · user `36112` · 2025-01-20

Yes!

That is largely the greatness of the Monster Die, I feel -- without it, you can "lock down" the situations more easily.  With it, you can never be too sure, and requires you to figure out which risks you want to take at which times.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-01-20

Anthony is right. When you play with the monster dice, you need greater margins on your defense. Note that the rotation sides on the monster dice may also mean monsters move into Grimheim. So when you are playing with the monster dice, try to defend 1 step further away from Grimheim, if possible.

---

Do they move clockwise or counter clockwise, or the action just doesnt happen?

**#6** · user `36112` · 2026-01-13

Only monsters adjacent to heroes rotate.

## Can Alva choose between different upgraded bows?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-18

Hi! All heroes have 2 discoverable Main Weapons, but may only use 1. When you find a new one, it permanently replaces the old one

## Can a location be also a forest?
*3 posts · started by ThomasWillinger on 2025-01-17* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3442494)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1281886` · 2025-01-17

There are several areas that are locations wich look like also be forests, like "witch cabin".

Are these just locations or also forests?

Thanks, Tom

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-17

Hi Tom. A location is on or more areas with a name. Those areas are normal areas with normal terrain types. All three single-area locations (Temple Ruins, Robber Camp, and Witch Cabin) are forests.

## Abilities on Equipment, static or apply only to attack?
*3 posts · started by SlippyBG on 2025-01-15* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3441629)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1317806` · 2025-01-15 *(edited)*

Hi

Played my first game today. Alva has an upgraded bow that lets her roll another dice when she rolls a Rune (assuming that’s what the axe symbol means in this context).

It’s worded as “whenever you roll”.

So does it apply to any roll you make, for example rolling dice from her throwing knives card?
Or is it only applied to dice rolled when you actually use the weapon?

Cheers!

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-16

Hi Maykel,

it always applies. The Main Weapon is usually considered part of the character itself, and their effects are usually such that they always apply, unless stated specifically that they only apply to "attack actions".

## Finkel's hero ability timing
*5 posts · started by pietu85 on 2025-01-13* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3440043)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `95899` · 2025-01-13

Finkel's ability says:
"For each Rune you roll, add 1 mana to Fireball"
When attacking, do I get this mana immediately after rolling the dice? May I use the mana gained this way to affect the outcome of the same attack, for example with Lightining Rod, which allows me to spend mana for extra damage?

Also, am I right to assume that Finkel's mana-gain works with all dice rolls, not only with attack actions? 🙂

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-13

Yes in both cases! You gain the mana immediately when you till the runes. Hypothetically, if Finkel has "Perfect Aim" and could re-roll all misses, he would first gain mana for each rolled rune, and then re-roll those runs, possibly earning more mana. And Lightning Rod is awesome, but remember he has to add mana for each additional damage he wants to deal. This includes Fireball level 2, where he deals 1 damage to all adjacent areas. He must spend 1 mana for each monster he wants to deal extra damage to.

Yes, because it is triggered on what you roll, and even if you reroll dice, they are still rolled 🙂

## Wrecking Ball

## Can I play a card during the End of Turn?
*3 posts · started by Doujou on 2025-01-06* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3436069)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `3067184` · 2025-01-07

As subject says. 

I was playing Bjorn and drew a card (Burning Arrow) that let's me:

"Deal 1 damage to a monster within attack range, or 2 damage if that monster stands in a forest."

My understanding is this is separate damage outside of my attack action. Is End of Turn still during my turn and thus able to play this card before the "official" end of my turn?

I had a skeleton next to me I used 2 of these cards on earlier in my turn and drew a 3rd during my draw step and it's kill that skeleton before he hits me. Hoping this is legal!?

Thanks!

---
**#2** · user `36112` · 2025-01-07

I don't believe so.  Once you start going down the end of turn steps (Reset, Upgrade, etc), you can no longer perform any actions - be they Free or otherwise.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-01-07

Anthony is right. The action phase is over when you get to the End of Turn sequence.

---

## Last turn?
*2 posts · started by NateTGreat on 2025-01-06* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3435759)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1694971` · 2025-01-06

Is the last turn when the stone moves to the last space on the time track, or is it when the stone moves off the last space of the time track?

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#2** · user `430700` · 2025-01-06

The monster turn progresses the time marker to the last space on the last turn of the game. If the monsters do not succeed to raze Freyja's well on that turn, the heroes win. So the heroes will not play any turn when there time marker is on the last space. Their last turn is on the next-to-last space.

---

🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430700` · 2025-01-06

You are right, they are limited, and that's why they use yellow markers instead of green ones. Because you could add green markers to cards with the focus action.

## What is considered an attack action? ✅
*5 posts · started by NateTGreat on 2025-01-06* — [link](https://boardgamegeek.com/thread/3435487)

📌 OP<br>**#1** · user `1694971` · 2025-01-06

Are Bjorn's throwing axes considered an attack action? Or is just doing the attack action considered an attack action. I'm wondering for the sake of using Bjorn's event card Master Shot, which adds 2 damage to 'this attack action'.

---
**#2** · user `1694971` · 2025-01-06

I think i just answered my own question from page 6. 'Free actions never count as attack actions.' So I assume using throwing axes is not an attack action, since it's a free action.

---
🎲 **DESIGNER — confirmed**<br>**#3** · user `430994` · 2025-01-06

> ↳ *Replying to #2 (user `1694971`):* I think i just answered my own question from page 6. 'Free actions never count as attack actions.' So I assume using throwing axes is not an attack action, since it's a free action.

> [q="NateTGreat"]I think i just answered my own question from page 6. 'Free actions never count as attack actions.' So I assume using throwing axes is not an attack action, since it's a free action. [/q]
> Correct.
> Only when you use your red action marker on attack or use a card that specifically gives you an 'attack action'. Throwing Axes is not giving you an attack action. It does however roll dice, so you can use cards that manipulate that, such as Perfect Aim and Piercing Arrows.
> Cheers!

---
